const LG={seriea:{n:“Serie A”,fl:“🇮🇹”},premierleague:{n:“Premier League”,fl:“🏴󠁧󠁢󠁥󠁮󠁧󠁿”},laliga:{n:“La Liga”,fl:“🇪🇸”},bundesliga:{n:“Bundesliga”,fl:“🇩🇪”},ligue1:{n:“Ligue 1”,fl:“🇫🇷”}};
const P={bg:”#080C14”,c1:”#0D1321”,c2:”#151D2E”,c3:”#1B2540”,bd:”#263354”,tx:”#EDF2FC”,td:”#8B9DC3”,tm:”#4F6289”,ac:”#00E5A0”,a2:”#00B4D8”,a3:”#F5A623”,dg:”#FF4757”,w:”#2ED573”,dr:”#F5A623”,lo:”#FF4757”,purple:”#A78BFA”,pink:”#F472B6”};

// ═══════ ADVANCED MATH ENGINE v2 ═══════
// Dixon-Coles + Bayesian Shrinkage + Time-Decay + Form Weighting

function poiP(l,k){if(l<=0)return k===0?1:0;let p=-l+k*Math.log(l);for(let i=2;i<=k;i++)p-=Math.log(i);return Math.exp(p);}
function poiCum(l,k){let s=0;for(let i=0;i<=k;i++)s+=poiP(l,i);return Math.min(1,s);}

// Weighted average: v/g where g is sum of weights (hwg or awg)
function wav(v,wg){return wg>0?v/wg:0;}
function av(v,g){return g>0?v/g:0;}

// Bayesian shrinkage: with few games trust league avg more
// k=8: at 8 weighted games, 50/50 split between team and league
function shrink(teamAvg,leagueAvg,weightedGames,k=8){
const w=weightedGames/(weightedGames+k);
return w*teamAvg+(1-w)*leagueAvg;
}

// Form factor from last 5: returns multiplier [0.85..1.15]
// Uses goal difference for nuance, not just W/D/L
function formFactor(last5){
if(!last5||!last5.length)return 1.0;
const weights=[1,1.5,2,2.5,3];
const n=Math.min(last5.length,5);
let score=0,totalW=0;
for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
const w=weights[n-1-i]||1;
const r=last5[last5.length-n+i];
const res=r.r||r;
// W=1, D=0.4, L=0 base; plus small GD bonus
const gd=r.gd||0;
const base=res===‘W’?1:res===‘D’?0.4:0;
const gdBonus=Math.max(-0.15,Math.min(0.15,gd*0.05));
score+=(base+gdBonus)*w;
totalW+=w;
}
const normalized=totalW>0?score/totalW:0.5;
// Map to [0.85..1.15] — enough to matter, not enough to dominate
return 0.85+normalized*0.30;
}

// Advanced lambda calculation
function calcLambdas(sH,sA,avgHG,avgAG,rho,nM){
// Time-weighted averages (data already weighted during preprocessing)
const rawHAtt=wav(sH.hgf,sH.hwg);
const rawHDef=wav(sH.hga,sH.hwg);
const rawAAtt=wav(sA.agf,sA.awg);
const rawADef=wav(sA.aga,sA.awg);

// Bayesian shrinkage toward league mean
const hAtt=shrink(rawHAtt,avgHG,sH.hwg,8);
const hDef=shrink(rawHDef,avgAG,sH.hwg,10);
const aAtt=shrink(rawAAtt,avgAG,sA.awg,8);
const aDef=shrink(rawADef,avgHG,sA.awg,10);

// Attack/defense strength ratios
const aStrH=hAtt/(avgHG||1.3);
const dWeakA=aDef/(avgAG||1.0);
const aStrA=aAtt/(avgAG||1.0);
const dWeakH=hDef/(avgHG||1.3);

let lH=aStrH*dWeakA*(avgHG||1.3);
let lA=aStrA*dWeakH*(avgAG||1.0);

// Form factor (home form for home team, away form for away)
const fH=formFactor(sH.l5h&&sH.l5h.length?sH.l5h:sH.l5);
const fA=formFactor(sA.l5a&&sA.l5a.length?sA.l5a:sA.l5);
lH*=fH; lA*=fA;

// Clamp
lH=Math.max(0.25,Math.min(4.5,lH));
lA=Math.max(0.15,Math.min(3.5,lA));

return{lH,lA,fH,fA,rawHAtt,rawHDef,rawAAtt,rawADef,hAtt,hDef,aAtt,aDef};
}

// Dixon-Coles matrix with empirical rho
function dcMatrix(lH,lA,rho,maxG=8){
const m=[];
for(let i=0;i<=maxG;i++){m[i]=[];for(let j=0;j<=maxG;j++)m[i][j]=poiP(lH,i)*poiP(lA,j);}

// Dixon-Coles tau corrections for (0,0),(1,0),(0,1),(1,1)
const r=rho||0;
m[0][0]*=Math.max(0.001,1-lH*lA*r);
m[1][0]*=Math.max(0.001,1+lA*r);
m[0][1]*=Math.max(0.001,1+lH*r);
m[1][1]*=Math.max(0.001,1-r);

// Normalize
let tot=0;
for(let i=0;i<=maxG;i++)for(let j=0;j<=maxG;j++)tot+=m[i][j];
if(tot>0&&Math.abs(tot-1)>0.001)for(let i=0;i<=maxG;i++)for(let j=0;j<=maxG;j++)m[i][j]/=tot;
return m;
}

function mxCalc(lH,lA,rho){return dcMatrix(lH,lA,rho);}

// ═══ xG MODEL — for goals only ═══
// Step 1-3 already computed in data (xgFH, xgAH, xgFA, xgAA, mO25)
// This function computes lambdas + market calibration
function calcXgLambdas(sH,sA){
// Insufficient data check
if((sH.xgNH||0)<5||(sA.xgNA||0)<5)return null;

// Step 3: Lambda = average of xGF and xGA
const lH=Math.max(0.01,((sH.xgFH||0)+(sA.xgAA||0))/2);
const lA=Math.max(0.01,((sA.xgFA||0)+(sH.xgAH||0))/2);
const lT=lH+lA;

// Step 4: Poisson P(Under 2.5)
const pU25_raw=Math.exp(-lT)*(1+lT+lT*lT/2);
const pO25_raw=1-pU25_raw;

// Step 5: GG/NG
const pGG=(1-Math.exp(-lH))*(1-Math.exp(-lA));

// Step 6: Market calibration
const avgMktOdds=((sH.mO25||2)+(sA.mO25||2))/2;
const pMarket=avgMktOdds>0?1/avgMktOdds:0.5;
const pO25_final=pO25_raw*0.65+pMarket*0.35;
const pU25_final=1-pO25_final;

// Form factor for display
const fH=formFactor(sH.l5h&&sH.l5h.length?sH.l5h:sH.l5);
const fA=formFactor(sA.l5a&&sA.l5a.length?sA.l5a:sA.l5);

return{lH,lA,lT,pO25_raw,pU25_raw,pO25:pO25_final,pU25:pU25_final,pGG,pNG:1-pGG,fH,fA,pMarket,avgMktOdds};
}

function mkts(mx){let h=0,d=0,a=0,o15=0,o25=0,o35=0,o45=0,gg=0,mg01=0,mg12=0,mg23=0,mg34=0,mg45=0;
for(let i=0;i<mx.length;i++)for(let j=0;j<mx[i].length;j++){const p=mx[i][j],t=i+j;
if(i>j)h+=p;else if(i===j)d+=p;else a+=p;if(t>1.5)o15+=p;if(t>2.5)o25+=p;if(t>3.5)o35+=p;if(t>4.5)o45+=p;
if(i>0&&j>0)gg+=p;if(t<=1)mg01+=p;if(t>=1&&t<=2)mg12+=p;if(t>=2&&t<=3)mg23+=p;if(t>=3&&t<=4)mg34+=p;if(t>=4&&t<=5)mg45+=p;}
return{“1”:h,X:d,“2”:a,“1X”:h+d,“X2”:d+a,“12”:h+a,O15:o15,U15:1-o15,O25:o25,U25:1-o25,O35:o35,U35:1-o35,O45:o45,U45:1-o45,GG:gg,NG:1-gg,M01:mg01,M12:mg12,M23:mg23,M34:mg34,M45:mg45};}

// Compute league home/away averages for any stat from all team data
function lgAvgSplit(ts,hKey,aKey){
let sH=0,sA=0,wH=0,wA=0;
Object.values(ts).forEach(s=>{sH+=s[hKey];wH+=s.hwg;sA+=s[aKey];wA+=s.awg;});
return{h:wH>0?sH/wH:1,a:wA>0?sA/wA:1};
}

// Expected stat using strength/weakness model (same approach as goals)
// hMade=team home made, aConceded=away team conceded away, lgH=league avg home, lgA=league avg away
// Plus shrinkage + form factor
function expStat(sH,sA,ts,hMadeKey,hConcKey,aMadeKey,aConcKey,formH,formA){
const lg=lgAvgSplit(ts,hMadeKey,aMadeKey);

// Raw weighted averages
const rawHAtt=wav(sH[hMadeKey],sH.hwg);    // home team attack (stat made at home)
const rawAConc=wav(sA[aConcKey],sA.awg);    // away team defense weakness (stat conceded away)
const rawAAtt=wav(sA[aMadeKey],sA.awg);     // away team attack (stat made away)
const rawHConc=wav(sH[hConcKey],sH.hwg);    // home team defense weakness (stat conceded at home)

// Shrinkage toward league mean
const hAtt=shrink(rawHAtt,lg.h,sH.hwg,8);
const aConc=shrink(rawAConc,lg.h,sA.awg,10);  // conceded away vs league home avg
const aAtt=shrink(rawAAtt,lg.a,sA.awg,8);
const hConc=shrink(rawHConc,lg.a,sH.hwg,10);  // conceded at home vs league away avg

// Strength/weakness ratios
const hAttStr=lg.h>0?hAtt/lg.h:1;
const aDefWeak=lg.h>0?aConc/lg.h:1;
const aAttStr=lg.a>0?aAtt/lg.a:1;
const hDefWeak=lg.a>0?hConc/lg.a:1;

// Expected = attack_strength × defense_weakness × league_baseline
let eH=hAttStr*aDefWeak*lg.h;
let eA=aAttStr*hDefWeak*lg.a;

// Apply form factor
eH*=formH; eA*=formA;

// Clamp to reasonable values
eH=Math.max(0.1,eH); eA=Math.max(0.1,eA);

return{eH,eA,t:eH+eA};
}

// Normal CDF approximation (Abramowitz & Stegun)
function normCDF(x){
if(x<-8)return 0;if(x>8)return 1;
const a1=0.254829592,a2=-0.284496736,a3=1.421413741,a4=-1.453152027,a5=1.061405429,p2=0.3275911;
const sign=x<0?-1:1;const z=Math.abs(x)/Math.SQRT2;
const t=1/(1+p2*z);const y=1-((((a5*t+a4)*t+a3)*t+a2)*t+a1)*t*Math.exp(-z*z);
return 0.5*(1+sign*y);
}

// P(Over X.5) using Poisson: P(X > floor(line)) = 1 - P(X <= floor(line))
function pOverPoi(lambda,line){return 1-poiCum(lambda,Math.floor(line));}

// Generate O/U lines using Poisson model (lambda = expected value)
function genLines(expected,leagueSD,step,isTeam){
// Find center line (nearest X.5)
const center=Math.round(expected)-0.5;
const lines=[];
for(let i=-2;i<=2;i++){
const line=Math.max(0.5, center+i*step);
const pOv=pOverPoi(expected,line);
if(pOv>0.02&&pOv<0.98){
lines.push({line,over:pOv,under:1-pOv});
}
}
const seen=new Set();
const unique=lines.filter(l=>{const k=l.line.toFixed(1);if(seen.has(k))return false;seen.add(k);return true;});
return unique.slice(0,5);
}

// Stat definitions with distribution type and step
const STAT_CFG={
tiri:{label:“Tiri Totali”,code:“xTS”,step:1,stepI:1,sdKey:“sdSh”,icon:“🎯”,accent:”#3B82F6”,bg:”#1a2744”,bg2:”#0f1a33”,desc:“Previsione tiri basata su intensità offensiva, permeabilità difensiva e ritmo”},
tiriPorta:{label:“Tiri in Porta”,code:“xTP”,step:1,stepI:1,sdKey:“sdSth”,icon:“🥅”,accent:”#8B5CF6”,bg:”#1f1a44”,bg2:”#14102e”,desc:“Previsione tiri in porta basata su precisione offensiva e qualità difensiva”},
corner:{label:“Corner”,code:“xC”,step:1,stepI:1,sdKey:“sdC”,icon:“📐”,accent:”#F97316”,bg:”#2d1f0a”,bg2:”#1a1208”,desc:“Previsione corner basata su pressione offensiva e difesa avversaria”},
falli:{label:“Falli”,code:“xF”,step:1,stepI:1,sdKey:“sdF”,icon:“⚠️”,accent:”#EF4444”,bg:”#2d0a0a”,bg2:”#1a0808”,desc:“Previsione falli basata su statistiche squadre, stile gioco e arbitro”},
cartellini:{label:“Cartellini Gialli”,code:“xY”,step:1,stepI:1,sdKey:“sdY”,icon:“🟨”,accent:”#F59E0B”,bg:”#2d2408”,bg2:”#1a1505”,desc:“Previsione cartellini basata su aggressività, falli attesi e tendenze arbitro”},
};

// ═══ VALUE INDICATOR ═══
// edge = distanza dalla soglia 50/50 → più è alta, più il modello è convinto
function valueTag(prob){
const edge=Math.abs(prob-0.5);
if(edge>=0.18)return{label:“⭐ TOP”,color:”#FFD700”,bg:”#FFD70022”};
if(edge>=0.12)return{label:“💎 VALUE”,color:”#22C55E”,bg:”#22C55E18”};
if(edge>=0.06)return{label:“✓ OK”,color:”#3B82F6”,bg:”#3B82F618”};
return{label:”—”,color:”#64748B”,bg:“transparent”};
}

// Compact threshold pill with value badge + fair odds
function ThPill({line,over,under}){
const bestP=Math.max(over,under);
const vt=valueTag(bestP);
const fairO=over>0.02?(1/over):99;
const fairU=under>0.02?(1/under):99;
return <div style={{textAlign:“center”,padding:“5px 4px”,borderRadius:7,minWidth:58,flex:“1 0 auto”,position:“relative”,
border:`2px solid ${over>=0.5?P.ac+"55":P.a2+"55"}`,background:over>=0.5?P.ac+“08”:P.a2+“08”}}>
{vt.label!==”—”&&<span style={{position:“absolute”,top:-8,right:-5,padding:“1px 4px”,borderRadius:4,background:vt.bg,border:`1px solid ${vt.color}55`,fontSize:7,fontWeight:800,color:vt.color,whiteSpace:“nowrap”}}>{vt.label}</span>}
<div style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:600,color:P.tx}}>{line.toFixed(1)}</div>
<div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:P.ac}}>O {(over*100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
<div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:P.a2}}>U {(under*100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
<div style={{fontSize:8,color:P.tm,marginTop:1}}>{fairO.toFixed(2)} / {fairU.toFixed(2)}</div>

  </div>;
}

function quickLambdas(sH,sA,ld){
const xg=calcXgLambdas(sH,sA);
if(xg)return{lH:xg.lH,lA:xg.lA,xg};
return calcLambdas(sH,sA,ld.avgHG||1.3,ld.avgAG||1.0,ld.rho||0,ld.nM||200);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════
EXCEL PARSER — reads uploaded .xlsx and builds same data structure
═══════════════════════════════════════════ */
const NM={
“AC Milan”:“Milan”,“Inter Milan”:“Inter”,“Hellas Verona”:“Verona”,
“Brighton & Hove Albion”:“Brighton”,“Leeds United”:“Leeds”,“Manchester City”:“Man City”,
“Manchester United”:“Man United”,“Newcastle United”:“Newcastle”,“Nottingham Forest”:“Nott’m Forest”,
“Tottenham Hotspur”:“Tottenham”,“West Ham United”:“West Ham”,“Wolverhampton Wanderers”:“Wolves”,
“Athletic Bilbao”:“Ath Bilbao”,“Atletico Madrid”:“Ath Madrid”,“Celta Vigo”:“Celta”,
“Espanyol”:“Espanol”,“Rayo Vallecano”:“Vallecano”,“Real Betis”:“Betis”,
“Real Oviedo”:“Oviedo”,“Real Sociedad”:“Sociedad”,
“1899 Hoffenheim”:“Hoffenheim”,“Bayer Leverkusen”:“Leverkusen”,“Borussia Dortmund”:“Dortmund”,
“Borussia Monchengladbach”:“M’gladbach”,“Cologne”:“FC Koln”,“Eintracht Frankfurt”:“Ein Frankfurt”,
“Mainz 05”:“Mainz”,“St. Pauli”:“St Pauli”,“Havre AC”:“Le Havre”,“Paris Saint-Germain”:“Paris SG”,
};
const nm=n=>NM[n]||n;
const LGCFG={
seriea:{ms:“seriea”,cs:“calendarioseriea”,rs:“arbitriseriea”,ss:“classificaseriea”},
premierleague:{ms:“premierleague”,cs:“calendariopremierleague”,rs:“arbitripremierleague”,ss:“classificapremierleague”},
laliga:{ms:“laliga”,cs:“calendariolaliga”,rs:“arbitrilaliga”,ss:“classificalaliga”},
bundesliga:{ms:“bundesliga”,cs:“calendariobundesliga”,rs:“arbitribundesliga”,ss:“classificabundesliga”},
ligue1:{ms:“ligue1”,cs:“calendarioligue1”,rs:“arbitriligue1”,ss:“classificaligue1”},
};
const DK=0.97;

function matchRefName(short,fulls){
const sp=short.trim().split(/\s+/);if(sp.length<2)return null;
const last=sp[sp.length-1].toLowerCase(),ini=sp[0][0].toLowerCase();
return fulls.find(fn=>{const fp=fn.trim().split(/\s+/);return fp.length>=2&&fp[fp.length-1].toLowerCase()===last&&fp[0][0].toLowerCase()===ini;})||null;
}

function parseExcelFile(wb){
const sheets=wb.SheetNames;
const out={};
for(const[key,cfg] of Object.entries(LGCFG)){
if(!sheets.includes(cfg.ms))continue;
const mRows=XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(wb.Sheets[cfg.ms])||[];
// Referee names from ref sheet
const rRows=sheets.includes(cfg.rs)?XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(wb.Sheets[cfg.rs])||[]:[];
const refFullNames=rRows.filter(r=>r.Referee).map(r=>String(r.Referee));
const hasRef=mRows.length>0&&mRows[0].Referee!==undefined;

```
// Parse matches
const matches=[];const refMD={};
const si=v=>{const n=Number(v);return isNaN(n)?0:Math.round(n);};
mRows.forEach(r=>{
  if(!r.HomeTeam||r.FTHG==null)return;
  const m={h:String(r.HomeTeam),a:String(r.AwayTeam),gh:si(r.FTHG),ga:si(r.FTAG),r:String(r.FTR||''),
    sh:si(r.HS),sa:si(r.AS),sth:si(r.HST),sta:si(r.AST),fh:si(r.HF),fa:si(r.AF),
    ch:si(r.HC),ca:si(r.AC),yh:si(r.HY),ya:si(r.AY),rh:si(r.HR),ra:si(r.AR)};
  if(hasRef&&r.Referee){
    const full=matchRefName(String(r.Referee),refFullNames);
    if(full){if(!refMD[full])refMD[full]=[];refMD[full].push({h:m.h,a:m.a,fh:m.fh,fa:m.fa,yh:m.yh,ya:m.ya,rh:m.rh,ra:m.ra,gh:m.gh,ga:m.ga});}
  }
  matches.push(m);
});
const N=matches.length;if(N===0)continue;

// Count home/away per team
const allT=[...new Set(matches.flatMap(m=>[m.h,m.a]))];
const hTot={},aTot={};allT.forEach(t=>{hTot[t]=0;aTot[t]=0;});
matches.forEach(m=>{hTot[m.h]++;aTot[m.a]++;});

// Build weighted stats
const ts={};
allT.forEach(t=>{ts[t]={hg:0,ag:0,hwg:0,awg:0,hgf:0,hga:0,agf:0,aga:0,hsh:0,hsha:0,ash:0,asha:0,
  hsth:0,hstha:0,asth:0,astha:0,hfh:0,hfha:0,afh:0,afha:0,hch:0,hcha:0,ach:0,acha:0,
  hyh:0,hyha:0,ayh:0,ayha:0,hrh:0,hrha:0,arh:0,arha:0,l5:[],l5h:[],l5a:[]};});
const hIdx={},aIdx={};allT.forEach(t=>{hIdx[t]=0;aIdx[t]=0;});
let lgHW=0,lgAW=0,lgTW=0,lgFW=0,lgYW=0,lgRW=0,lgCW=0;
const stTotals={sh:[],sth:[],f:[],y:[],c:[]};

matches.forEach(m=>{
  const h=m.h,a=m.a;if(!ts[h]||!ts[a])return;
  const wH=Math.pow(DK,hTot[h]-1-hIdx[h]);const wA=Math.pow(DK,aTot[a]-1-aIdx[a]);
  hIdx[h]++;aIdx[a]++;
  const s=ts[h],sa2=ts[a];
  s.hg++;sa2.ag++;s.hwg+=wH;sa2.awg+=wA;
  [['hgf','gh'],['hga','ga'],['hsh','sh'],['hsha','sa'],['hsth','sth'],['hstha','sta'],
   ['hfh','fh'],['hfha','fa'],['hch','ch'],['hcha','ca'],['hyh','yh'],['hyha','ya'],['hrh','rh'],['hrha','ra']].forEach(([k1,k2])=>{s[k1]+=m[k2]*wH;});
  [['agf','ga'],['aga','gh'],['ash','sa'],['asha','sh'],['asth','sta'],['astha','sth'],
   ['afh','fa'],['afha','fh'],['ach','ca'],['acha','ch'],['ayh','ya'],['ayha','yh'],['arh','ra'],['arha','rh']].forEach(([k1,k2])=>{sa2[k1]+=m[k2]*wA;});
  const wAv=(wH+wA)/2;
  lgHW+=m.gh*wAv;lgAW+=m.ga*wAv;lgTW+=wAv;
  lgFW+=(m.fh+m.fa)*wAv;lgYW+=(m.yh+m.ya)*wAv;lgRW+=(m.rh+m.ra)*wAv;lgCW+=(m.ch+m.ca)*wAv;
  stTotals.sh.push(m.sh+m.sa);stTotals.sth.push(m.sth+m.sta);
  stTotals.f.push(m.fh+m.fa);stTotals.y.push(m.yh+m.ya);stTotals.c.push(m.ch+m.ca);
  const hR=m.r==='H'?'W':m.r==='D'?'D':'L';const aR=m.r==='A'?'W':m.r==='D'?'D':'L';
  const gdH=m.gh-m.ga,gdA=m.ga-m.gh;
  s.l5.push({r:hR,o:a,s:`${m.gh}-${m.ga}`,gd:gdH});
  sa2.l5.push({r:aR,o:h,s:`${m.ga}-${m.gh}`,gd:gdA});
  s.l5h.push({r:hR,o:a,s:`${m.gh}-${m.ga}`,gd:gdH});
  sa2.l5a.push({r:aR,o:h,s:`${m.ga}-${m.gh}`,gd:gdA});
});
allT.forEach(t=>{ts[t].l5=ts[t].l5.slice(-5);ts[t].l5h=ts[t].l5h.slice(-5);ts[t].l5a=ts[t].l5a.slice(-5);});

// Rho estimation
const avgHR=matches.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.gh,0)/N,avgAR=matches.reduce((s,m)=>s+m.ga,0)/N;
const n00=matches.filter(m=>m.gh===0&&m.ga===0).length;
const n11=matches.filter(m=>m.gh===1&&m.ga===1).length;
const e00=poiP(avgHR,0)*poiP(avgAR,0)*N,e11=poiP(avgHR,1)*poiP(avgAR,1)*N;
let rho=e00>0&&e11>0?Math.max(-0.2,Math.min(0.05,-0.03*(n00/e00-1)+0.03*(n11/e11-1))):-0.1;

// SDs
const calcSD=arr=>{if(arr.length<2)return 3;const m=arr.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/arr.length;return Math.sqrt(arr.reduce((s,v)=>s+(v-m)*(v-m),0)/(arr.length-1));};

// Calendar
const calRows=sheets.includes(cfg.cs)?XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(wb.Sheets[cfg.cs])||[]:[];
const cal=calRows.filter(r=>r.Column2).map(r=>({d:String(r.Column1||''),h:nm(String(r.Column2)),a:nm(String(r.Column3||''))}));

// Referees
const ref=rRows.filter(r=>r.Referee).map(r=>{
  const cpg=String(r['Cards per game']||'0');
  const mr=cpg.match(/([\d.]+)\s*\(([\d.]+)\s*\/\s*([\d.]+)\)/);
  const rn=String(r.Referee);
  const rd={n:rn,g:Number(r.Games)||0,ty:Number(r.Column1)||0,tr:Number(r['_1'])||0,
    cpg:mr?parseFloat(mr[1]):0,ypg:mr?parseFloat(mr[2]):0,rpg:mr?parseFloat(mr[3]):0};
  if(refMD[rn]){const rms=refMD[rn];const ng=rms.length;
    rd.fpg=+(rms.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.fh+x.fa,0)/ng).toFixed(2);
    rd.fhpg=+(rms.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.fh,0)/ng).toFixed(2);rd.fapg=+(rms.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.fa,0)/ng).toFixed(2);
    rd.yhpg=+(rms.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.yh,0)/ng).toFixed(2);rd.yapg=+(rms.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.ya,0)/ng).toFixed(2);
    rd.rhpg=+(rms.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.rh,0)/ng).toFixed(2);rd.rapg=+(rms.reduce((s,x)=>s+x.ra,0)/ng).toFixed(2);
    rd.hist=rms.map(x=>({h:x.h,a:x.a,f:x.fh+x.fa,y:x.yh+x.ya}));
  }
  return rd;
});

// Standings
const stRows=sheets.includes(cfg.ss)?XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(wb.Sheets[cfg.ss])||[]:[];
const st=stRows.filter(r=>r.Team).map(r=>({p:Number(r.Pos)||0,t:nm(String(r.Team)),pl:Number(r.Pld)||0,
  w:Number(r.W)||0,d:Number(r.D)||0,l:Number(r.L)||0,gd:r['+/-']!=null?Number(r['+/-']):0,
  pts:Number(r.Pts)||0,f:String(r.Form||'')}));

out[key]={ts,cal,ref,st,
  avgHG:+(lgHW/lgTW).toFixed(4),avgAG:+(lgAW/lgTW).toFixed(4),
  avgF:+(lgFW/lgTW).toFixed(2),avgY:+(lgYW/lgTW).toFixed(2),avgR:+(lgRW/lgTW).toFixed(2),avgC:+(lgCW/lgTW).toFixed(2),
  nM:N,rho:+rho.toFixed(4),
  sdSh:+calcSD(stTotals.sh).toFixed(2),sdSth:+calcSD(stTotals.sth).toFixed(2),
  sdF:+calcSD(stTotals.f).toFixed(2),sdY:+calcSD(stTotals.y).toFixed(2),sdC:+calcSD(stTotals.c).toFixed(2),
};
```

}
return out;
}

// Severity classification
function sevClass(idx){if(idx<80)return{l:“PERMISSIVO”,c:”#22C55E”};if(idx<90)return{l:“SOTTO MEDIA”,c:”#3B82F6”};
if(idx<=110)return{l:“NELLA MEDIA”,c:”#F59E0B”};if(idx<=120)return{l:“SOPRA MEDIA”,c:”#F97316”};return{l:“SEVERO”,c:”#EF4444”};}

// Components
function FB({f}){if(!f||!f.length)return null;const items=typeof f===‘string’?f.split(’’).map(c=>({r:c})):f;
return <div style={{display:“flex”,gap:4,flexWrap:“wrap”}}>{items.map((x,i)=>{
const c=x.r||x;const col=c===‘W’?P.w:c===‘D’?P.dr:P.lo;
return <div key={i} style={{display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,alignItems:“center”,gap:2}}>
<span style={{width:26,height:26,borderRadius:6,display:“inline-flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“center”,fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,background:col,color:”#fff”}}>{c===‘W’?‘V’:c===‘D’?‘P’:‘S’}</span>
{x.o&&<span style={{fontSize:9,color:P.td,maxWidth:50,textAlign:“center”,overflow:“hidden”,textOverflow:“ellipsis”,whiteSpace:“nowrap”}}>{x.o}</span>}
{x.s&&<span style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:600,color:P.tx}}>{x.s}</span>}

</div>})}</div>;}

function SB({label,vA,vB,cA=P.ac,cB=P.a2}){const mx=Math.max(vA,vB,0.01);
return <div style={{marginBottom:10}}><div style={{display:“flex”,justifyContent:“space-between”,fontSize:11,color:P.td,marginBottom:3}}>
<span>{vA.toFixed(1)}</span><span style={{fontWeight:600}}>{label}</span><span>{vB.toFixed(1)}</span></div>

<div style={{display:"flex",height:8,gap:3,borderRadius:4,overflow:"hidden"}}>
<div style={{flex:vA/mx,background:cA,borderRadius:"4px 0 0 4px",transition:"flex 0.5s"}}/>
<div style={{flex:vB/mx,background:cB,borderRadius:"0 4px 4px 0",transition:"flex 0.5s"}}/></div></div>;}

function PBr({label,prob,color=P.ac}){return <div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:8,marginBottom:6}}>
<span style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td,width:80,textAlign:“right”,flexShrink:0}}>{label}</span>

<div style={{flex:1,height:20,background:P.c3,borderRadius:10,overflow:"hidden",position:"relative"}}>
<div style={{width:`${Math.min(prob*100,100)}%`,height:"100%",background:`linear-gradient(90deg,${color}88,${color})`,borderRadius:10,transition:"width 0.6s"}}/>
<span style={{position:"absolute",right:6,top:2,fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"#fff"}}>{(prob*100).toFixed(1)}%</span></div></div>;}

function Cd({children,style={},onClick}){const[hv,setHv]=useState(false);
return <div onClick={onClick} onMouseEnter={()=>onClick&&setHv(true)} onMouseLeave={()=>setHv(false)}
style={{background:P.c1,border:`1px solid ${hv?P.ac:P.bd}`,borderRadius:12,padding:18,
…(onClick?{cursor:“pointer”,transform:hv?“translateY(-2px)”:“none”,transition:“all 0.2s”}:{}),
…style}}>{children}</div>;}

function teamStatRow(s,def){
const hv=def.h(s),av2=def.a(s),hg=s[def.hg]||1,ag=s[def.ag]||1;
return{tot:hv+av2,totH:hv,totA:av2,avgT:(hv+av2)/(hg+ag),avgH:hv/hg,avgA:av2/ag};
}

function TeamSection({ld}){
const[tab,setTab]=useState(“dettagli”);
const[selTeam,setSelTeam]=useState(””);

const allTeams=Object.keys(ld.ts||{}).sort();
const ts=ld.ts||{};

const scopeLabels={tot:“Totale”,totH:“Totale Casa”,totA:“Totale Trasferta”,avgT:“Media Totale”,avgH:“Media Casa”,avgA:“Media Trasferta”};
const statLabels=STAT_DEFS.reduce((o,d)=>{o[d.k]=d.l;return o;},{});

return <>
{/* Sub-tabs */}
<div style={{display:“flex”,gap:8,marginBottom:16}}>
{[[“confronto”,“Confronto”],[“dettagli”,“Dettagli”],[“classifiche”,“Classifiche”]].map(([k,lb])=>
<button key={k} onClick={()=>setTab(k)}
style={{flex:1,padding:“12px 8px”,borderRadius:10,border:“none”,fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,cursor:“pointer”,transition:“all 0.2s”,
background:tab===k?P.ac:”#1a3a2a”,color:tab===k?”#0B0F19”:P.ac}}>
{lb}
</button>
)}
</div>

```
{/* CONFRONTO */}
{tab==="confronto"&&<Cd>
  <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr auto 1fr",gap:12,alignItems:"center",marginBottom:20}}>
    <div>
      <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,textAlign:"center",marginBottom:6}}>Casa:</div>
      <select value={selH} onChange={e=>setSelH(e.target.value)}
        style={{width:"100%",background:P.c3,border:`2px solid ${P.ac}44`,color:P.tx,padding:"12px 10px",borderRadius:10,fontSize:13}}>
        <option value="">Seleziona squadra...</option>
        {allTeams.map(t=><option key={t} value={t}>{t}</option>)}

    </div>
    <div style={{width:50,height:50,borderRadius:25,background:P.ac,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",fontSize:16,fontWeight:900,color:"#0B0F19"}}>VS</div>
    <div>
      <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,textAlign:"center",marginBottom:6}}>Trasferta:</div>

        <th style={{padding:"10px 8px",textAlign:"left",color:"#0B0F19",fontWeight:700,fontSize:11}}>STATISTICA</th>
        <th style={{padding:"10px 8px",textAlign:"center",color:"#0B0F19",fontWeight:700,fontSize:11}}>{selH} (C)</th>
        <th style={{padding:"10px 8px",textAlign:"center",color:"#0B0F19",fontWeight:700,fontSize:11}}>{selA} (T)</th>
      </tr></thead>
      <tbody>{STAT_DEFS.map((def,i)=>{
        const rH=teamStatRow(ts[selH],def), rA=teamStatRow(ts[selA],def);
        const vH=def.k.includes("Sub")?rH.avgH:rH.avgH, vA=def.k.includes("Sub")?rA.avgA:rA.avgA;
        const better=vH>vA;
        return <tr key={def.k} style={{borderBottom:`1px solid ${P.bd}22`,background:i%2===0?"transparent":P.c3+"44"}}>
          <td style={{padding:"8px",fontWeight:600,fontSize:11,color:P.td,textTransform:"uppercase"}}>{def.l}</td>
          <td style={{padding:"8px",textAlign:"center",fontWeight:700,color:better?P.ac:P.a3}}>{vH.toFixed(2)}</td>
          <td style={{padding:"8px",textAlign:"center",fontWeight:700,color:!better?P.ac:P.a3}}>{vA.toFixed(2)}</td>
        </tr>;
      })}</tbody>
    </table>
  </div>:<div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:30,color:P.td}}>Seleziona entrambe le squadre</div>}
</Cd>}

{/* DETTAGLI */}
{tab==="dettagli"&&<>
  <Cd style={{marginBottom:14}}>
    <div style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,marginBottom:8}}>Squadra:</div>
    <select value={selTeam} onChange={e=>setSelTeam(e.target.value)}
      style={{width:"100%",background:P.c3,border:`2px solid ${P.ac}44`,color:P.tx,padding:"12px 14px",borderRadius:10,fontSize:14}}>

          </div>

              <th style={{padding:"10px 8px",textAlign:"center",color:"#0B0F19",fontWeight:700,fontSize:11}}>MEDIA TOT</th>
              <th style={{padding:"10px 8px",textAlign:"center",color:"#0B0F19",fontWeight:700,fontSize:11}}>MEDIA CASA</th>
              <th style={{padding:"10px 8px",textAlign:"center",color:"#0B0F19",fontWeight:700,fontSize:11}}>MEDIA TRASF.</th>
            </tr></thead>

              const r=teamStatRow(s,def);
              return <tr key={def.k} style={{borderBottom:`1px solid ${P.bd}22`,background:i%2===0?"transparent":P.c3+"44"}}>
                <td style={{padding:"8px",fontWeight:600,fontSize:11,color:P.td,textTransform:"uppercase"}}>{def.l}</td>
                <td style={{padding:"8px",textAlign:"center",fontWeight:700,color:def.c}}>{r.avgT.toFixed(2)}</td>
                <td style={{padding:"8px",textAlign:"center",fontWeight:700,color:"#3B82F6"}}>{r.avgH.toFixed(2)}</td>
                <td style={{padding:"8px",textAlign:"center",fontWeight:700,color:"#F97316"}}>{r.avgA.toFixed(2)}</td>
              </tr>;
            })}</tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </Cd>
    </>;})()}
  </>:<div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:30,color:P.td}}>Seleziona una squadra per vedere le statistiche</div>}
</>}

{/* CLASSIFICHE */}
{tab==="classifiche"&&<Cd>
  <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:10,marginBottom:16}}>
    <select value={rkScope} onChange={e=>setRkScope(e.target.value)}
      style={{background:P.c3,border:`2px solid ${P.ac}44`,color:P.tx,padding:"12px 10px",borderRadius:10,fontSize:13}}>
      {Object.entries(scopeLabels).map(([k,lb])=><option key={k} value={k}>{lb}</option>)}
    </select>
    <select value={rkStat} onChange={e=>setRkStat(e.target.value)}
      style={{background:P.c3,border:`2px solid ${P.ac}44`,color:P.tx,padding:"12px 10px",borderRadius:10,fontSize:13}}>
      {STAT_DEFS.map(d=><option key={d.k} value={d.k}>{d.l}</option>)}
    </select>
  </div>
  <div style={{fontSize:15,fontWeight:700,marginBottom:12}}>{statLabels[rkStat]||rkStat}</div>
  {(()=>{
    const def=STAT_DEFS.find(d=>d.k===rkStat);
    if(!def)return null;
    const ranked=allTeams.map(t=>{const r=teamStatRow(ts[t],def);return{t,v:r[rkScope]||0};})
      .sort((a,b)=>b.v-a.v);
    return ranked.map((r,i)=>{
      const isTop3=i<3;
      return <div key={r.t} style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",padding:"12px 14px",marginBottom:6,
        background:isTop3?P.ac+"15":P.c3,borderRadius:10,border:isTop3?`1px solid ${P.ac}33`:`1px solid ${P.bd}22`}}>
        <span style={{width:32,fontSize:16,fontWeight:800,color:isTop3?P.ac:P.td}}>{i+1}</span>
        <span style={{flex:1,fontWeight:600,fontSize:14}}>{r.t}</span>
        <div style={{textAlign:"right"}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:800,color:isTop3?P.ac:def.c}}>{r.v.toFixed(2)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>;
    });
  })()}
</Cd>}
```

</>;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════
REFEREE SECTION - ENHANCED
═══════════════════════════════════════════ */
function RefSection({ld}){
const[sel,setSel]=useState(””);
const[tab,setTab]=useState(“medie”);
const[rankStat,setRankStat]=useState(“ypg”);
const refs=ld.ref||[];
const ref=refs.find(r=>r.n===sel);
const avgF=ld.avgF||26, avgY=ld.avgY||4, avgR=ld.avgR||0.15;

// Index calculation: (ref_stat / league_avg) * 100
const calcIdx=(refVal,leagueVal)=>leagueVal>0?(refVal/leagueVal)*100:100;

return <>
{/* Selector */}
<Cd style={{marginBottom:14}}>
<div style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,marginBottom:8}}>SELEZIONA ARBITRO:</div>
<select value={sel} onChange={e=>{setSel(e.target.value);setTab(“medie”);}}
style={{width:“100%”,background:P.c3,border:`2px solid ${P.ac}44`,color:P.tx,padding:“12px 14px”,borderRadius:10,fontSize:14,cursor:“pointer”}}>
<option value="">– Seleziona un arbitro –</option>
{refs.sort((a,b)=>a.n.localeCompare(b.n)).map(r=><option key={r.n} value={r.n}>{r.n}</option>)}
</select>
</Cd>

```
{ref&&<>
  {/* Tabs */}
  <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,marginBottom:14}}>
    {[["medie","Medie"],["indici","Indici & Analisi"],["storico",`Storico (${ref.g})`],["classifiche","Classifiche"]].map(([k,lb])=>
      <button key={k} onClick={()=>setTab(k)}
        style={{flex:1,padding:"10px 8px",borderRadius:10,border:"none",fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,cursor:"pointer",transition:"all 0.2s",
          background:tab===k?P.ac:"#1a3a2a",color:tab===k?"#0B0F19":P.ac}}>
        {lb}
      </button>
    )}
  </div>

  {/* MEDIE TAB */}
  {tab==="medie"&&<Cd>
    <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:16}}>
      <div style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td}}>Partite arbitrate:</div>
      <div style={{fontSize:28,fontWeight:800,color:P.ac}}>{ref.g}</div>
    </div>
    <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:12}}>
      {/* Cartellini Gialli */}
      <div style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#F59E0B33,#F59E0B11)",borderRadius:12,padding:16,textAlign:"center"}}>
        <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.a3,textTransform:"uppercase",marginBottom:4}}>Cartellini Gialli</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:32,fontWeight:800,color:P.a3}}>{ref.ypg.toFixed(2)}</div>
        {ref.yhpg!=null&&<div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"center",gap:12,marginTop:8}}>
          <span style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>🏠 {ref.yhpg.toFixed(2)}</span>
          <span style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>✈️ {ref.yapg.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </div>}
      </div>
      {/* Cartellini Rossi */}
      <div style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#EF444433,#EF444411)",borderRadius:12,padding:16,textAlign:"center"}}>
        <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.dg,textTransform:"uppercase",marginBottom:4}}>Cartellini Rossi</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:32,fontWeight:800,color:P.dg}}>{ref.rpg.toFixed(2)}</div>
        {ref.rhpg!=null&&<div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"center",gap:12,marginTop:8}}>
          <span style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>🏠 {ref.rhpg.toFixed(2)}</span>
          <span style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>✈️ {ref.rapg.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </div>}
      </div>
      {/* Falli */}
      <div style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#22C55E33,#22C55E11)",borderRadius:12,padding:16,textAlign:"center"}}>
        <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.w,textTransform:"uppercase",marginBottom:4}}>Falli / Partita</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:32,fontWeight:800,color:P.w}}>{ref.fpg!=null?ref.fpg.toFixed(2):"N/A"}</div>
        {ref.fhpg!=null&&<div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"center",gap:12,marginTop:8}}>
          <span style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>🏠 {ref.fhpg.toFixed(2)}</span>
          <span style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>✈️ {ref.fapg.toFixed(2)}</span>
        </div>}
      </div>
      {/* Media Campionato */}
      <div style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#3B82F633,#3B82F611)",borderRadius:12,padding:16,textAlign:"center"}}>
        <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:"#3B82F6",textTransform:"uppercase",marginBottom:4}}>Media Campionato</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:14,color:P.td,marginTop:8}}>Falli: {avgF.toFixed(2)}</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:14,color:P.td}}>Gialli: {avgY.toFixed(2)}</div>
        <div style={{fontSize:14,color:P.td}}>Rossi: {avgR.toFixed(2)}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </Cd>}

  {/* INDICI & ANALISI TAB */}
  {tab==="indici"&&<Cd>
    {(()=>{
      const idxY=calcIdx(ref.ypg,avgY);
      const idxR=calcIdx(ref.rpg,avgR);
      const idxF=ref.fpg!=null?calcIdx(ref.fpg,avgF):null;
      const idxGen=idxF!=null?(idxY*0.4+idxF*0.4+idxR*0.2):(idxY*0.7+idxR*0.3);
      const sevY=sevClass(idxY),sevR=sevClass(idxR),sevGen=sevClass(idxGen);
      const sevF=idxF!=null?sevClass(idxF):null;

      const diffY=((ref.ypg-avgY)/avgY*100).toFixed(0);
      const diffF=ref.fpg!=null?((ref.fpg-avgF)/avgF*100).toFixed(0):null;

      return <>
        {/* Index cards */}
        {[["Indice Disciplinare",idxY,sevY],
          ...(idxF!=null?[["Indice Falli",idxF,sevF]]:[]),
          ["Indice Generale",idxGen,sevGen]].map(([lb,val,sev])=>
          <div key={lb} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:16,marginBottom:12,background:P.c3,borderRadius:12,border:`1px solid ${sev.c}33`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td,fontWeight:600}}>{lb}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:36,fontWeight:800,color:sev.c,margin:"4px 0"}}>{val.toFixed(2)}</div>
            <div style={{display:"inline-block",padding:"4px 16px",borderRadius:20,background:sev.c+"22",color:sev.c,fontSize:12,fontWeight:700}}>{sev.l}</div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Legend */}
        <div style={{padding:14,background:P.c3,borderRadius:10,marginBottom:16}}>
          <div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:13,marginBottom:8}}>LEGENDA INDICI</div>
          <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:4,fontSize:12}}>
            {[["< 80","Permissivo","#22C55E"],["80-90","Sotto Media","#3B82F6"],["90-110","Nella Media","#F59E0B"],["110-120","Sopra Media","#F97316"],["> 120","Severo","#EF4444"]].map(([r,l,c])=>
              <div key={l} style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:6}}>
                <span style={{width:10,height:10,borderRadius:5,background:c,flexShrink:0}}/>
                <span style={{color:P.td}}><b style={{color:P.tx}}>{r}:</b> {l}</span>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Performance Analysis */}
        <div style={{padding:16,background:P.c3,borderRadius:12,marginBottom:14}}>
          <div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:15,marginBottom:12,borderBottom:`2px solid ${P.ac}`,paddingBottom:6}}>Analisi Performance</div>
          <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:12}}>
            {[["FALLI",ref.fpg,avgF,P.w],["GIALLI",ref.ypg,avgY,P.a3],["ROSSI",ref.rpg,avgR,P.dg]].map(([lb,val,avg,c])=>
              val!=null&&<div key={lb} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,background:P.c2,borderRadius:8}}>
                <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.tm,textTransform:"uppercase"}}>{lb}</div>
                <div style={{fontSize:24,fontWeight:800,color:c}}>{val.toFixed(2)}</div>
                <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>Media: {avg.toFixed(2)}</div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Insights */}
        <div style={{padding:16,background:P.c3,borderRadius:12}}>
          <div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:14,marginBottom:10}}>⚖️ DISCIPLINA</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td,lineHeight:1.8}}>
            {diffF!=null&&<div>Arbitro {Number(diffF)<0?"tendenzialmente permissivo":"tendenzialmente severo"} ({diffF>0?"+":""}{diffF}% falli vs media)</div>}

            {ref.ypg>0&&ref.fpg>0&&<div>{((ref.ypg/ref.fpg)*100).toFixed(0)}% dei falli portano ad ammonizione</div>}
          </div>
          <div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:14,marginTop:14,marginBottom:6}}>🟨 CARTELLINI</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td,lineHeight:1.8}}>
            <div>{ref.ypg.toFixed(1)} ammonizioni per gara ({diffY>0?"+":""}{diffY}% vs media)</div>
            <div>{ref.rpg>0?"Frequenza espulsioni: "+ref.rpg.toFixed(2)+"/partita":"Bassa frequenza espulsioni: "+ref.rpg.toFixed(2)+"/partita"}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </>;
    })()}
  </Cd>}

  {/* STORICO TAB */}
  {tab==="storico"&&<Cd>
    {ref.hist&&ref.hist.length>0?<>
      <div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:16,marginBottom:12,borderBottom:`2px solid ${P.ac}`,paddingBottom:6}}>Storico Partite Arbitrate</div>

          <div style={{width:40,height:40,borderRadius:20,background:P.ac+"22",display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",fontSize:14,fontWeight:800,color:P.ac,flexShrink:0}}>{m.f}</div>
          <div style={{flex:1,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",gap:8}}>

            <span style={{color:P.tm,fontSize:12,fontWeight:600}}>vs</span>
            <span style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:13,textAlign:"left",flex:1}}>{m.a}</span>
          </div>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.a3,fontWeight:600,flexShrink:0}}>🟨 {m.y}</div>

      <p style={{fontSize:12,color:P.tm}}>Disponibile per Premier League (dati arbitro nei match).</p>

      return <div key={r.n} style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",padding:"12px 14px",marginBottom:6,

        <div style={{textAlign:"right"}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:800,color:isTop3?P.a3:P.ac}}>{val.toFixed(2)}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>per partita</div>
        </div>

    })}
  </Cd>}

}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════
MATCH ANALYSIS
═══════════════════════════════════════════ */
function Analysis({fix,ld,onBack}){
const{h:home,a:away}=fix;
const{ts,ref:refs,avgHG,avgAG,avgF,avgY,avgR,st}=ld;
const sH=ts[home],sA=ts[away];
const[selRef,setSelRef]=useState(””);

if(!sH||!sA)return <div><button onClick={onBack} style={bbS}>← Indietro</button>
<Cd><p style={{color:P.dg}}>Dati non trovati per {home} vs {away}.</p></Cd></div>;

const hAtt=av(sH.hgf,sH.hg),hDef=av(sH.hga,sH.hg),aAtt=av(sA.agf,sA.ag),aDef=av(sA.aga,sA.ag);

// ═══ xG MODEL for goals ═══
const xg = calcXgLambdas(sH, sA);
// Fallback to old model if insufficient xG data
const lambdasOld = calcLambdas(sH, sA, avgHG, avgAG, ld.rho||0, ld.nM);
const lH = xg ? xg.lH : lambdasOld.lH;
const lA = xg ? xg.lA : lambdasOld.lA;
const fH = xg ? xg.fH : lambdasOld.fH;
const fA = xg ? xg.fA : lambdasOld.fA;
const mx=dcMatrix(lH,lA,ld.rho||0),mk=mkts(mx);
// Calibrated O/U 2.5 from xG model (overrides raw Poisson)
if(xg){mk.O25=xg.pO25;mk.U25=xg.pU25;mk.GG=xg.pGG;mk.NG=xg.pNG;}

const ref=refs.find(r=>r.n===selRef);
const rIdx=ref?(ref.cpg/((avgY||4))):1;

const ev={
tiri:expStat(sH,sA,ts,‘hsh’,‘hsha’,‘ash’,‘asha’,fH,fA),
tiriPorta:expStat(sH,sA,ts,‘hsth’,‘hstha’,‘asth’,‘astha’,fH,fA),
falli:expStat(sH,sA,ts,‘hfh’,‘hfha’,‘afh’,‘afha’,fH,fA),
corner:expStat(sH,sA,ts,‘hch’,‘hcha’,‘ach’,‘acha’,fH,fA),
cartellini:expStat(sH,sA,ts,‘hyh’,‘hyha’,‘ayh’,‘ayha’,fH,fA),
};

// Apply referee modifier
if(ref){
const fIdx=ref.fpg!=null?ref.fpg/(avgF||26):rIdx;
const yIdx=ref.ypg/(avgY||4);
ev.falli.eH*=fIdx;ev.falli.eA*=fIdx;ev.falli.t=ev.falli.eH+ev.falli.eA;
ev.cartellini.eH*=yIdx;ev.cartellini.eA*=yIdx;ev.cartellini.t=ev.cartellini.eH+ev.cartellini.eA;
}

const stH=st.find(s=>s.t===home),stA=st.find(s=>s.t===away);
// stat labels now in STAT_CFG
const radar=[{stat:“Gol”,A:hAtt,B:aAtt},{stat:“Tiri”,A:wav(sH.hsh,sH.hwg)/4,B:wav(sA.ash,sA.awg)/4},
{stat:“T.Porta”,A:wav(sH.hsth,sH.hwg)/2,B:wav(sA.asth,sA.awg)/2},{stat:“Corner”,A:wav(sH.hch,sH.hwg)/2,B:wav(sA.ach,sA.awg)/2},
{stat:“Difesa”,A:Math.max(0,3-hDef),B:Math.max(0,3-aDef)}];

return <div><button onClick={onBack} style={bbS}>← Torna al Calendario</button>

```
{/* Header */}
<Cd style={{background:`linear-gradient(135deg,${P.c1},${P.c2})`,marginBottom:14,textAlign:"center"}}>
  <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm,textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:"0.08em",marginBottom:10}}>{fix.d}</div>
  <div style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",gap:20,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
    <div style={{textAlign:"right",flex:1,minWidth:100}}>
      <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:800}}>{home}</div>
      {stH&&<div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>#{stH.p} · {stH.pts} pts</div>}
      {sH.l5h&&sH.l5h.length>0&&<div style={{marginTop:6,display:"flex",justifyContent:"flex-end"}}><FB f={sH.l5h}/></div>}
    </div>
    <div style={{fontSize:28,fontWeight:900,color:P.ac,padding:"8px 18px",background:P.c3,borderRadius:10}}>VS</div>
    <div style={{textAlign:"left",flex:1,minWidth:100}}>
      <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:800}}>{away}</div>
      {stA&&<div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td}}>#{stA.p} · {stA.pts} pts</div>}
      {sA.l5a&&sA.l5a.length>0&&<div style={{marginTop:6}}><FB f={sA.l5a}/></div>}
    </div>
  </div>
</Cd>

{/* Model Info */}
<div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(140px,1fr))",gap:8,marginBottom:14}}>
  <div style={{padding:"10px 12px",borderRadius:8,background:"#0d2818",border:"1px solid #22C55E33",textAlign:"center"}}>
    <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm,textTransform:"uppercase"}}>Modello</div>
    <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:P.ac}}>Dixon-Coles</div>
  </div>
  <div style={{padding:"10px 12px",borderRadius:8,background:P.c3,textAlign:"center"}}>
    <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>Shrinkage k</div>
    <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:P.a2}}>Att:8 Dif:10</div>
  </div>
  <div style={{padding:"10px 12px",borderRadius:8,background:fH>=1?"#0d2818":"#2d1215",border:`1px solid ${fH>=1?"#22C55E33":"#EF444433"}`,textAlign:"center"}}>
    <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>Forma {home}</div>
    <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:fH>=1?P.w:P.dg}}>{fH>=1?"+":""}{((fH-1)*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
  </div>
  <div style={{padding:"10px 12px",borderRadius:8,background:fA>=1?"#0d2818":"#2d1215",border:`1px solid ${fA>=1?"#22C55E33":"#EF444433"}`,textAlign:"center"}}>
    <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>Forma {away}</div>
    <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:fA>=1?P.w:P.dg}}>{fA>=1?"+":""}{((fA-1)*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
  </div>
</div>

{/* ═══ BLOCCO 1: BANNER FAVORITO + STATO DI FORMA ═══ */}
{(()=>{
  // Compute form metrics from last 5 match data
  const parseScore=(s)=>{const p=(s||"").split("-").map(Number);return{gf:p[0]||0,ga:p[1]||0};};
  const formRatio=(matches,n)=>{
    const slice=matches.slice(-Math.min(n,matches.length));
    if(!slice.length)return 1;
    const gf=slice.reduce((s,m)=>s+parseScore(m.s).gf,0);
    const ga=slice.reduce((s,m)=>s+parseScore(m.s).ga,0);
    return ga>0?gf/ga:(gf>0?3:1);
  };
  const points5=(matches)=>{
    const slice=matches.slice(-5);
    return slice.reduce((s,m)=>s+(m.r==='W'?3:m.r==='D'?1:0),0);
  };
  const avgGols=(matches)=>{
    const slice=matches.slice(-5);
    if(!slice.length)return{gf:0,ga:0};
    const gf=slice.reduce((s,m)=>s+parseScore(m.s).gf,0)/slice.length;
    const ga=slice.reduce((s,m)=>s+parseScore(m.s).ga,0)/slice.length;
    return{gf:+gf.toFixed(2),ga:+ga.toFixed(2)};
  };

  const fH3=formRatio(sH.l5h||sH.l5,3), fH5=formRatio(sH.l5h||sH.l5,5);
  const fA3=formRatio(sA.l5a||sA.l5,3), fA5=formRatio(sA.l5a||sA.l5,5);
  // Form 10 approximated from season weighted data
  const fH10=wav(sH.hgf,sH.hwg)/(wav(sH.hga,sH.hwg)||0.5);
  const fA10=wav(sA.agf,sA.awg)/(wav(sA.aga,sA.awg)||0.5);
  const ptsH=points5(sH.l5h||sH.l5), ptsA=points5(sA.l5a||sA.l5);
  const avgH=avgGols(sH.l5h||sH.l5), avgA=avgGols(sA.l5a||sA.l5);
  const trendH=fH3>fH5*1.05?"📈":fH3<fH5*0.95?"📉":"➡️";
  const trendA=fA3>fA5*1.05?"📈":fA3<fA5*0.95?"📉":"➡️";

  // Banner
  const xgDiff=lH-lA;
  const absD=Math.abs(xgDiff);
  const fav=xgDiff>0?home:away;
  const favForm=xgDiff>0?fH:fA;
  const favTrend=xgDiff>0?trendH:trendA;
  const lvl=absD>1.2?"nettamente favorito":absD>0.6?"favorito":absD>0.25?"leggermente favorito":"match equilibrato";
  const isEq=absD<=0.25;

  return <>
    {/* Banner Favorito */}
    <div style={{padding:"14px 18px",borderRadius:12,marginBottom:14,
      background:isEq?"linear-gradient(135deg,#1a2744,#142033)":`linear-gradient(135deg,${xgDiff>0?P.ac+"18":P.a2+"18"},${P.c2})`,
      border:`1px solid ${isEq?P.bd:xgDiff>0?P.ac+"44":P.a2+"44"}`,
      display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",gap:14,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
      <span style={{fontSize:20}}>{isEq?"⚖️":"🔥"}</span>
      <span style={{fontSize:15,fontWeight:700,color:isEq?P.a3:xgDiff>0?P.ac:P.a2}}>
        {isEq?"Match equilibrato":`${fav} ${lvl}`}
      </span>
      <span style={{fontSize:15,fontWeight:800,color:P.tx}}>({xgDiff>0?"+":""}{xgDiff.toFixed(2)} xG)</span>
      {!isEq&&<span style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td}}>{favTrend} {fav} {favForm>=1?"in forma":"in calo"}</span>}
    </div>

    {/* Stato di Forma Avanzato */}
    <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:10,marginBottom:14}}>
      {[[home,sH,fH3,fH5,fH10,ptsH,avgH,trendH,P.ac,"l5h"],[away,sA,fA3,fA5,fA10,ptsA,avgA,trendA,P.a2,"l5a"]].map(([name,s,f3,f5,f10,pts,ag,trend,color,formKey])=>
        <Cd key={name} style={{padding:14}}>
          <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center",marginBottom:10}}>
            <span style={{fontSize:15,fontWeight:800}}>{name}</span>
            <span style={{fontSize:22}}>{trend}</span>
          </div>
          <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr",gap:6,marginBottom:10}}>
            {[["Form 3",f3,color],["Form 5",f5,color],["Form 10",f10,color],["Punti 5",null,null]].map(([lb,val,c],i)=>
              <div key={lb} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"6px 4px",borderRadius:6,background:P.c3}}>
                <div style={{fontSize:9,color:P.tm}}>{lb}</div>
                {i<3?<div style={{fontSize:16,fontWeight:800,color:val>=1?P.w:P.dg}}>{val.toFixed(2)}</div>
                  :<div style={{fontSize:16,fontWeight:800,color:P.a3}}>{pts}/15</div>}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.td,textAlign:"center"}}>
            Ultime 5 {formKey==="l5h"?"casa":"trasferta"}: media gol <b style={{color:P.tx}}>{ag.gf}</b> / subiti <b style={{color:P.tx}}>{ag.ga}</b>
          </div>
        </Cd>
      )}
    </div>

    {/* Legend */}
    <div style={{textAlign:"center",fontSize:11,color:P.tm,marginBottom:14,padding:"8px 12px",background:P.c2,borderRadius:8}}>
      Form {">"} 1.00 = squadra in forma (segna più e/o subisce meno della media) | 📈 = trend positivo | 📉 = trend negativo | ➡️ = stabile
    </div>
  </>;
})()}

{/* Value Indicator Legend */}
<div style={{padding:"10px 14px",borderRadius:10,marginBottom:14,background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1a1a2e,#16213e)",border:`1px solid ${P.bd}44`}}>
  <div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:P.tx,marginBottom:6,textAlign:"center"}}>💰 INDICATORE DI VALORE</div>
  <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,justifyContent:"center",flexWrap:"wrap",marginBottom:6}}>

      <div key={lb} style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:4,padding:"3px 8px",borderRadius:6,background:c+"15",border:`1px solid ${c}33`}}>
        <span style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:800,color:c}}>{lb}</span>
        <span style={{fontSize:9,color:P.td}}>{desc}</span>
      </div>
    )}
  </div>
  <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm,textAlign:"center"}}>
    Edge = distanza dalla soglia 50/50. <b style={{color:P.td}}>Fair Odds</b> = quota equa (1/prob) — confronta con il tuo bookmaker per trovare valore!

<div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(310px,1fr))",gap:14}}>
  <Cd><h3 style={ctS}>📊 Confronto Statistiche</h3>

  <Cd><h3 style={ctS}>🎯 Profilo Squadre</h3>

  <Cd><h3 style={ctS}>🏆 Pronostico 1X2</h3>
    <div style={{display:"flex",gap:10,marginBottom:16}}>
      {[["1",home,P.ac],["X","Pareggio",P.a3],["2",away,P.a2]].map(([k,lb,c])=>{
        const p=mk[k]||0;
        const vt=valueTag(p);
        return <div key={k} style={{flex:1,textAlign:"center",padding:12,borderRadius:10,position:"relative",
          background:p===Math.max(mk["1"]||0,mk.X||0,mk["2"]||0)?c+"12":P.c3,
          border:`1px solid ${p===Math.max(mk["1"]||0,mk.X||0,mk["2"]||0)?c+"44":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
          {vt.label!=="—"&&<span style={{position:"absolute",top:-7,right:-4,padding:"1px 5px",borderRadius:4,background:vt.bg,border:`1px solid ${vt.color}55`,fontSize:7,fontWeight:800,color:vt.color}}>{vt.label}</span>}
          <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm,marginBottom:4}}>{lb}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:24,fontWeight:800,color:c}}>{(p*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.td,marginTop:2}}>Fair: {p>0.01?(1/p).toFixed(2):"—"}</div>
        </div>;
      })}
    </div>
    <h4 style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td,fontWeight:600,marginBottom:8}}>Doppia Chance</h4>
    {[["1X",mk["1X"],P.ac],["X2",mk["X2"],P.a2],["12",mk["12"],P.a3]].map(([lb,p,c])=>{
      const vt=valueTag(p||0);
      const fair=p>0.02?(1/p).toFixed(2):"—";
      return <div key={lb} style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:8,marginBottom:6}}>
        <div style={{flex:1}}><PBr label={lb} prob={p} color={c}/></div>
        <div style={{width:44,textAlign:"center",fontSize:9,color:P.tm}}>Fair: {fair}</div>
        {vt.label!=="—"&&<span style={{padding:"1px 5px",borderRadius:4,background:vt.bg,border:`1px solid ${vt.color}55`,fontSize:8,fontWeight:800,color:vt.color}}>{vt.label}</span>}
      </div>;
    })}
  </Cd>

  <Cd><h3 style={ctS}>📈 Over / Under Gol</h3>
    <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td,marginBottom:10}}>
      <div>λ Casa: {lH.toFixed(2)} · λ Trasf: {lA.toFixed(2)} · Gol Attesi: {(lH+lA).toFixed(2)}</div>
      <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm,marginTop:2}}>Modello xG Proxy + Calibrazione Mercato{xg?` · Odds medio O2.5: ${xg.avgMktOdds.toFixed(2)}`:""}</div>
    </div>
    {["1.5","2.5","3.5","4.5"].map(line=>{
      const k=line.replace(".","");
      const pOv=mk["O"+k]||0, pUn=mk["U"+k]||0;
      const bestP=Math.max(pOv,pUn);
      const vt=valueTag(bestP);
      const fairO=pOv>0.02?(1/pOv):99;
      const fairU=pUn>0.02?(1/pUn):99;
      return <div key={line} style={{display:"flex",gap:6,marginBottom:8,alignItems:"stretch"}}>
        <div style={{flex:1,padding:"8px 10px",borderRadius:8,textAlign:"center",
          background:pOv>=pUn?P.ac+"10":P.c3,border:`1px solid ${pOv>=pUn?P.ac+"33":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm}}>Over {line}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:700,color:pOv>=pUn?P.ac:P.td}}>{(pOv*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:9,color:P.tm}}>Fair: {fairO.toFixed(2)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style={{flex:1,padding:"8px 10px",borderRadius:8,textAlign:"center",
          background:pUn>pOv?P.a2+"10":P.c3,border:`1px solid ${pUn>pOv?P.a2+"33":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm}}>Under {line}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:700,color:pUn>pOv?P.a2:P.td}}>{(pUn*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:9,color:P.tm}}>Fair: {fairU.toFixed(2)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style={{width:52,display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",
          padding:"4px 2px",borderRadius:8,background:vt.bg,border:`1px solid ${vt.color}33`}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:9,fontWeight:800,color:vt.color,textAlign:"center",lineHeight:1.2}}>{vt.label}</div>
        </div>
      </div>;
    })}
  </Cd>

  <Cd><h3 style={ctS}>⚽ Goal / No Goal</h3>
    {(()=>{
      const pGG=mk.GG||0, pNG=mk.NG||0;
      const vtGG=valueTag(pGG);
      const fairGG=pGG>0.02?(1/pGG):99;
      const fairNG=pNG>0.02?(1/pNG):99;
      return <div style={{display:"flex",gap:10,marginBottom:16}}>
        <div style={{flex:1,textAlign:"center",padding:14,borderRadius:10,position:"relative",
          background:pGG>=pNG?P.ac+"12":P.c3,border:`1px solid ${pGG>=pNG?P.ac+"33":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
          {pGG>=pNG&&<span style={{position:"absolute",top:-8,left:"50%",transform:"translateX(-50%)",padding:"2px 10px",borderRadius:10,background:P.ac,fontSize:9,fontWeight:800,color:"#0B0F19"}}>FAVORITO</span>}
          <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.tm,marginTop:4}}>GOAL (GG)</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:28,fontWeight:800,color:P.ac}}>{(pGG*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.td}}>Entrambe segnano</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:9,color:P.tm,marginTop:2}}>Fair: {fairGG.toFixed(2)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style={{flex:1,textAlign:"center",padding:14,borderRadius:10,position:"relative",
          background:pNG>pGG?P.dg+"12":P.c3,border:`1px solid ${pNG>pGG?P.dg+"33":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
          {pNG>pGG&&<span style={{position:"absolute",top:-8,left:"50%",transform:"translateX(-50%)",padding:"2px 10px",borderRadius:10,background:P.dg,fontSize:9,fontWeight:800,color:"#fff"}}>FAVORITO</span>}
          <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.tm,marginTop:4}}>NO GOAL (NG)</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:28,fontWeight:800,color:P.dg}}>{(pNG*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.td}}>Almeno una non segna</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:9,color:P.tm,marginTop:2}}>Fair: {fairNG.toFixed(2)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style={{width:52,display:"flex",flexDirection:"column",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center",
          padding:"4px 2px",borderRadius:8,background:vtGG.bg,border:`1px solid ${vtGG.color}33`}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:9,fontWeight:800,color:vtGG.color,textAlign:"center",lineHeight:1.2}}>{vtGG.label}</div>
        </div>
      </div>;
    })()}
    <h4 style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td,fontWeight:600,marginBottom:8}}>Multigol</h4>
    {[["0-1","M01"],["1-2","M12"],["2-3","M23"],["3-4","M34"],["4-5","M45"]].map(([lb,k])=>
      <PBr key={k} label={lb} prob={mk[k]} color={P.a3}/>)}
  </Cd>

  {/* ═══ EXPECTED STATISTICS ═══ */}
  {/* Referee selector */}
  <Cd style={{gridColumn:"1 / -1"}}>
    <div style={{display:"flex",gap:10,alignItems:"center",flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
      <div style={{flex:1,minWidth:200}}>
        <div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:P.tm,marginBottom:4}}>⚖️ ARBITRO (OPZIONALE)</div>
        <select value={selRef} onChange={e=>setSelRef(e.target.value)}
          style={{width:"100%",background:P.c3,border:`2px solid ${P.ac}44`,color:P.tx,padding:"10px 12px",borderRadius:8,fontSize:13,cursor:"pointer"}}>
          <option value="">-- Seleziona arbitro --</option>
          {refs.sort((a,b)=>a.n.localeCompare(b.n)).map(r=><option key={r.n} value={r.n}>{r.n} ({r.cpg}/g)</option>)}
        </select>
      </div>
      {ref&&<div style={{flex:1,minWidth:200,padding:12,background:P.c3,borderRadius:8,fontSize:12}}>
        <div style={{fontWeight:700,color:P.tx,marginBottom:4}}>{ref.n}</div>
        <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
          <span style={{color:P.td}}>Falli/P: <b style={{color:P.a3}}>{ref.fpg!=null?ref.fpg.toFixed(1):"N/A"}</b> <span style={{color:P.tm}}>vs media {avgF.toFixed(1)}</span></span>
          <span style={{color:P.td}}>Gialli/P: <b style={{color:P.a3}}>{ref.ypg.toFixed(1)}</b> <span style={{color:P.tm}}>vs media {avgY.toFixed(1)}</span></span>
          <span style={{color:P.td}}>Rossi/P: <b style={{color:P.dg}}>{ref.rpg.toFixed(2)}</b></span>
          <span style={{color:P.td}}>Partite: <b>{ref.g}</b></span>
        </div>
        {ref.fpg!=null&&<div style={{marginTop:4,fontSize:11}}>
          <span style={{color:P.tm}}>Impatto Falli: </span><span style={{fontWeight:700,color:ref.fpg/avgF>1.05?P.dg:ref.fpg/avgF<0.95?P.w:P.a3}}>→ x{(ref.fpg/avgF).toFixed(2)}</span>
          <span style={{color:P.tm,marginLeft:8}}>Impatto Gialli: </span><span style={{fontWeight:700,color:ref.ypg/avgY>1.05?P.dg:ref.ypg/avgY<0.95?P.w:P.a3}}>→ x{(ref.ypg/avgY).toFixed(2)}</span>
        </div>}
      </div>}
    </div>
  </Cd>

  {Object.entries(ev).map(([key,e])=>{
    const cfg=STAT_CFG[key];
    if(!cfg)return null;
    const leagueSD=ld[cfg.sdKey]||3;
    const sdT=Math.sqrt(e.t);  // Poisson SD = sqrt(lambda)
    const sdI_H=Math.sqrt(e.eH);
    const sdI_A=Math.sqrt(e.eA);
    const linesT=genLines(e.t,leagueSD,cfg.step,false);
    const linesH=genLines(e.eH,leagueSD,cfg.stepI||1,true);
    const linesA=genLines(e.eA,leagueSD,cfg.stepI||1,true);
    // Ranges (±1.2 SD Poisson)
    const rngH=[Math.max(0,Math.floor(e.eH-1.2*sdI_H)),Math.ceil(e.eH+1.2*sdI_H)];
    const rngA=[Math.max(0,Math.floor(e.eA-1.2*sdI_A)),Math.ceil(e.eA+1.2*sdI_A)];
    const rngT=[Math.max(0,Math.floor(e.t-1.2*sdT)),Math.ceil(e.t+1.2*sdT)];
    // Is cartellini? Use cumulative 1+,2+,3+... format
    const isCards=key==="cartellini";
    // Cumulative probabilities for Poisson (for cards)
    const cumProbs=(lambda,max)=>{const arr=[];for(let k=1;k<=max;k++)arr.push({k,p:1-poiCum(lambda,k-1)});return arr;};

    return <Cd key={key} style={{gridColumn:"1 / -1",padding:0,overflow:"hidden"}}>
      {/* Header badge */}
      <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"12px 14px",background:`linear-gradient(135deg,${cfg.bg||P.c2},${cfg.bg2||P.c1})`}}>
        <div style={{display:"inline-block",padding:"4px 16px",borderRadius:20,background:cfg.accent||P.ac,fontSize:12,fontWeight:800,color:"#0B0F19",textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:"0.05em"}}>
          EXPECTED {cfg.label.toUpperCase()} ({cfg.code})
        </div>
        <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td,marginTop:6}}>{cfg.desc}</div>
      </div>

      {/* 3-column values: Casa | Totale | Trasferta */}
      <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr 1fr",gap:0,padding:"14px 14px 8px"}}>
        {/* Casa */}
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,borderRight:`1px solid ${P.bd}33`}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.ac}}>🏠 {home}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:32,fontWeight:800,color:P.ac,margin:"4px 0"}}>{e.eH.toFixed(1)}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>{cfg.unitH||cfg.label+" Attesi"}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td,marginTop:4}}>{rngH[0]} - {rngH[1]}</div>
        </div>
        {/* Totale */}
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,background:P.c3}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.a3}}>TOTALE PARTITA</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:36,fontWeight:800,color:P.a3,margin:"4px 0"}}>{e.t.toFixed(1)}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>{cfg.label} Attesi</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td,marginTop:4}}>{rngT[0]} - {rngT[1]}</div>
        </div>
        {/* Trasferta */}
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,borderLeft:`1px solid ${P.bd}33`}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.a2}}>✈️ {away}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:32,fontWeight:800,color:P.a2,margin:"4px 0"}}>{e.eA.toFixed(1)}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>{cfg.unitA||cfg.label+" Attesi"}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.td,marginTop:4}}>{rngA[0]} - {rngA[1]}</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div style={{padding:"8px 14px 14px"}}>
        {/* O/U TOTALE PARTITA */}
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:10}}>
          <span style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.a3,padding:"3px 12px",borderRadius:12,background:P.a3+"18"}}>O/U {cfg.label} Totale Partita</span>
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"flex",gap:4,marginBottom:14,flexWrap:"wrap",justifyContent:"center"}}>
          {linesT.map((ln,i)=><ThPill key={i} line={ln.line} over={ln.over} under={ln.under}/>)}
        </div>

        {/* O/U PER SQUADRA (or cumulative for cards) */}
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:10}}>
          <span style={{fontSize:11,fontWeight:700,color:P.td,padding:"3px 12px",borderRadius:12,background:P.c2}}>
            {isCards?"Probabilità Cartellini per Squadra":"O/U "+cfg.label+" per Squadra"}
          </span>
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:10}}>
          {/* Home team */}
          <div style={{padding:10,background:P.c2,borderRadius:8,border:`1px solid ${P.ac}22`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:P.ac,marginBottom:6}}>🏠 {home} ({cfg.code}: {e.eH.toFixed(1)})</div>
            {isCards?
              <div style={{display:"flex",gap:3,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
                {cumProbs(e.eH,5).map(c=><div key={c.k} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"4px 6px",borderRadius:6,flex:"1 0 auto",minWidth:40,
                  background:c.p>=0.5?P.ac+"15":P.c3,border:`1px solid ${c.p>=0.5?P.ac+"33":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
                  <div style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:600,color:P.tm}}>{c.k}+</div>
                  <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:c.p>=0.5?P.ac:P.td}}>{(c.p*100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
                </div>)}
              </div>
              :<div style={{display:"flex",gap:3,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
                {linesH.map((ln,i)=><ThPill key={i} line={ln.line} over={ln.over} under={ln.under}/>)}
              </div>
            }
          </div>
          {/* Away team */}
          <div style={{padding:10,background:P.c2,borderRadius:8,border:`1px solid ${P.a2}22`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:700,color:P.a2,marginBottom:6}}>✈️ {away} ({cfg.code}: {e.eA.toFixed(1)})</div>
            {isCards?
              <div style={{display:"flex",gap:3,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
                {cumProbs(e.eA,5).map(c=><div key={c.k} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"4px 6px",borderRadius:6,flex:"1 0 auto",minWidth:40,
                  background:c.p>=0.5?P.a2+"15":P.c3,border:`1px solid ${c.p>=0.5?P.a2+"33":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
                  <div style={{fontSize:10,fontWeight:600,color:P.tm}}>{c.k}+</div>
                  <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:c.p>=0.5?P.a2:P.td}}>{(c.p*100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
                </div>)}
              </div>
              :<div style={{display:"flex",gap:3,flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
                {linesA.map((ln,i)=><ThPill key={i} line={ln.line} over={ln.over} under={ln.under}/>)}
              </div>
            }
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Entrambi almeno (for cards) */}
        {isCards&&<div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:10,marginTop:10}}>
          <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,background:P.a3+"12",borderRadius:8,border:`1px solid ${P.a3}33`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm}}>Entrambi Almeno 1</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.td}}>Entrambe ricevono almeno 1 giallo</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:24,fontWeight:800,color:P.a3}}>{((1-poiP(e.eH,0))*(1-poiP(e.eA,0))*100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
          </div>
          <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,background:P.dg+"12",borderRadius:8,border:`1px solid ${P.dg}33`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm}}>Entrambi Almeno 2</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.td}}>Entrambe ricevono almeno 2 gialli</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:24,fontWeight:800,color:P.dg}}>{((1-poiP(e.eH,0)-poiP(e.eH,1))*(1-poiP(e.eA,0)-poiP(e.eA,1))*100).toFixed(0)}%</div>
          </div>
        </div>}

        {/* Range boxes */}
        <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr 1fr",gap:8,marginTop:12}}>
          <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:10,background:P.c2,borderRadius:8,border:`1px solid ${P.ac}22`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>Range {home}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:P.ac}}>{rngH[0]} - {rngH[1]}</div>
          </div>
          <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:10,background:P.c2,borderRadius:8,border:`1px solid ${P.a3}22`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>Range Totale</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:P.a3}}>{rngT[0]} - {rngT[1]}</div>
          </div>
          <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:10,background:P.c2,borderRadius:8,border:`1px solid ${P.a2}22`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>Range {away}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:P.a2}}>{rngA[0]} - {rngA[1]}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </Cd>;
  })}

  {/* ═══ BLOCCO 2: TOP 5 RISULTATI + MULTIGOL ═══ */}

  {/* Top 5 Risultati Più Probabili */}
  <Cd style={{gridColumn:"1 / -1"}}>
    {(()=>{
      const results=[];
      for(let i=0;i<=6;i++)for(let j=0;j<=6;j++){
        const p=mx[i]&&mx[i][j]?mx[i][j]:0;
        if(p>0)results.push({h:i,a:j,p,label:`${i}-${j}`,side:i>j?"Casa":i===j?"Pareggio":"Trasferta"});
      }
      results.sort((a,b)=>b.p-a.p);
      const top5=results.slice(0,5);
      return <>
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:12}}>
          <span style={{display:"inline-block",padding:"6px 20px",borderRadius:20,background:"#8B5CF6",fontSize:12,fontWeight:800,color:"#fff",textTransform:"uppercase"}}>Top 5 Risultati Più Probabili</span>
        </div>
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"10px 14px",background:P.c3,borderRadius:8,marginBottom:14,fontSize:13,color:P.td}}>
          <b style={{color:P.tx}}>Ricorda:</b> I primi 2-3 risultati hanno spesso % simili, considerali tutti come possibili esiti!
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"flex",gap:8,justifyContent:"center",flexWrap:"wrap"}}>
          {top5.map((r,i)=><div key={i} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"10px 14px",borderRadius:10,minWidth:70,
            background:i===0?"#8B5CF622":P.c3,border:i===0?`2px solid #8B5CF666`:`1px solid ${P.bd}33`}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm,fontWeight:700}}>#{i+1}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:24,fontWeight:800,color:r.side==="Casa"?P.ac:r.side==="Pareggio"?P.a3:P.a2}}>{r.label}</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:P.td}}>{(r.p*100).toFixed(1)}%</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>{r.side}</div>
          </div>)}
        </div>
      </>;
    })()}
  </Cd>

  {/* Multigol Totale Match */}
  <Cd style={{gridColumn:"1 / -1"}}>
    {(()=>{
      // Compute P(min <= total goals <= max) from matrix
      const mgP=(min,max)=>{
        let s=0;
        for(let i=0;i<=7;i++)for(let j=0;j<=7;j++){
          const t=i+j;
          if(t>=min&&t<=max&&mx[i]&&mx[i][j])s+=mx[i][j];
        }
        return s;
      };
      // Also 7+
      const mg7p=(()=>{let s=0;for(let i=0;i<=7;i++)for(let j=0;j<=7;j++){if((i+j)>=7&&mx[i]&&mx[i][j])s+=mx[i][j];}return s;})();

      const ranges=[
        ["1-2",1,2],["1-3",1,3],["1-4",1,4],["1-5",1,5],["1-6",1,6],
        ["2-3",2,3],["2-4",2,4],["2-5",2,5],["2-6",2,6],
        ["3-4",3,4],["3-5",3,5],["3-6",3,6],
        ["4-5",4,5],["4-6",4,6],["5-6",5,6],
      ];
      const items=ranges.map(([lb,mn,mx2])=>({lb,p:mgP(mn,mx2)}));
      items.push({lb:"7+",p:mg7p});

      return <>
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:12}}>
          <span style={{display:"inline-block",padding:"6px 20px",borderRadius:20,background:"#3B82F6",fontSize:12,fontWeight:800,color:"#fff",textTransform:"uppercase"}}>Multigol Totale Match</span>
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(4,1fr)",gap:6}}>
          {items.map((it,i)=>{
            const hot=it.p>=0.65;
            const pct=it.p*100;
            const bg=pct>=65?"#3B82F6":pct>=50?"#3B82F6CC":pct>=35?"#3B82F644":"transparent";
            const tx2=pct>=50?"#fff":pct>=35?P.tx:P.td;
            return <div key={it.lb} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"10px 4px",borderRadius:8,position:"relative",
              background:bg,border:`1px solid ${pct>=50?"#3B82F666":P.bd+"33"}`}}>
              {hot&&<span style={{position:"absolute",top:-6,right:-4,background:"#F59E0B",color:"#fff",fontSize:8,fontWeight:800,padding:"2px 5px",borderRadius:6}}>HOT</span>}
              <div style={{fontSize:12,color:tx2,fontWeight:600}}>{it.lb}</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,color:tx2}}>{pct.toFixed(0)}%</div>
            </div>;
          })}
        </div>
      </>;
    })()}
  </Cd>

  {/* Multigol Per Squadra */}
  <Cd style={{gridColumn:"1 / -1"}}>
    {(()=>{
      // P(min <= team goals <= max) using Poisson on individual lambda
      const teamMG=(lambda,ranges)=>ranges.map(([lb,mn,mx2])=>{
        let s=0;for(let k=mn;k<=mx2;k++)s+=poiP(lambda,k);
        return{lb,p:s};
      });
      const rangesTeam=[["0-1",0,1],["0-2",0,2],["1-2",1,2],["1-3",1,3],["2-3",2,3],["2-4",2,4],["2-5",2,5]];
      const mgH=teamMG(lH,rangesTeam);
      const mgA=teamMG(lA,rangesTeam);

      return <>
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",marginBottom:12}}>
          <span style={{display:"inline-block",padding:"6px 20px",borderRadius:20,background:P.ac,fontSize:12,fontWeight:800,color:"#0B0F19",textTransform:"uppercase"}}>Multigol Per Squadra</span>
        </div>
        <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr",gap:12}}>
          {[[home,mgH,lH,P.ac],[away,mgA,lA,P.a2]].map(([name,items,lambda,color])=>
            <div key={name} style={{padding:12,background:P.c2,borderRadius:10,border:`1px solid ${color}22`}}>
              <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color,marginBottom:8}}>Multigol {name}</div>
              <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fill,minmax(55px,1fr))",gap:4}}>
                {items.map((it,i)=>{
                  const pct=it.p*100;
                  const hot=pct>=60;
                  return <div key={it.lb} style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"6px 3px",borderRadius:6,
                    background:hot?color+"22":P.c3,border:`1px solid ${hot?color+"44":P.bd+"22"}`}}>
                    <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>{it.lb}</div>
                    <div style={{fontSize:15,fontWeight:800,color:hot?color:P.td}}>{pct.toFixed(0)}%</div>
                  </div>;
                })}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </>;
    })()}
  </Cd>

  {/* Matrix */}
  <Cd style={{gridColumn:"1 / -1"}}><h3 style={ctS}>🔢 Matrice Risultati Esatti</h3>
    <div style={{overflowX:"auto"}}><table style={{borderCollapse:"collapse",fontSize:12,width:"100%",maxWidth:600}}>
      <thead><tr><th style={mTh}>{home} vs {away}</th>
        {[0,1,2,3,4,5].map(j=><th key={j} style={mTh}>{j}</th>)}</tr></thead>
      <tbody>{[0,1,2,3,4,5].map(i=><tr key={i}><td style={{...mTd,fontWeight:700,color:P.ac}}>{i}</td>
        {[0,1,2,3,4,5].map(j=>{const p=mx[i][j]*100;return <td key={j} style={{...mTd,
          background:`rgba(0,229,160,${Math.min(p/15,0.6)})`,fontWeight:p>5?700:400,color:p>5?"#fff":P.td}}>{p.toFixed(1)}%</td>;})}</tr>)}</tbody>
    </table></div>
  </Cd>

  {/* ═══ BLOCCO 3: ANALISI FINALE MATCH + METRICHE ═══ */}
  {(()=>{
    // Top results from matrix
    const results=[];
    for(let i=0;i<=6;i++)for(let j=0;j<=6;j++){if(mx[i]&&mx[i][j]&&mx[i][j]>0)results.push({h:i,a:j,p:mx[i][j]});}
    results.sort((a,b)=>b.p-a.p);
    const top3=results.slice(0,3);
    const topResult=top3[0]||{h:0,a:0,p:0};

    // Key probabilities
    const o15=mk.O15||0, o25=mk.O25||0, o35=mk.O35||0;
    const gg=mk.GG||0, ng=mk.NG||0;

    // Best multigol (from matrix)
    const mgP2=(mn,mx2)=>{let s=0;for(let i=0;i<=7;i++)for(let j=0;j<=7;j++){const t=i+j;if(t>=mn&&t<=mx2&&mx[i]&&mx[i][j])s+=mx[i][j];}return s;};
    const mgRanges=[["1-2",1,2],["1-3",1,3],["2-3",2,3],["2-4",2,4],["2-5",2,5],["3-5",3,5],["3-6",3,6]];
    const bestMG=mgRanges.map(([lb,mn,mx2])=>({lb,p:mgP2(mn,mx2)})).sort((a,b)=>b.p-a.p)[0];

    // Expected stats summary
    const xgDiff=lH-lA;
    const fav=xgDiff>0?home:away;
    const favLambda=xgDiff>0?lH:lA;
    const undLambda=xgDiff>0?lA:lH;
    const lvl=Math.abs(xgDiff)>1.2?"nettamente favorita":Math.abs(xgDiff)>0.6?"favorita":Math.abs(xgDiff)>0.25?"leggermente favorita":"equilibrata";

    // Stile partita
    const totalFouls=ev.falli.t;
    const avgFoulsLg=ld.avgF||26;
    const stilePartita=totalFouls>avgFoulsLg*1.15?"Molto Fisica":totalFouls>avgFoulsLg*1.0?"Fisica":totalFouls>avgFoulsLg*0.85?"Normale":"Fluida";
    const stileColor=totalFouls>avgFoulsLg*1.15?P.dg:totalFouls>avgFoulsLg?P.a3:totalFouls>avgFoulsLg*0.85?P.td:P.ac;

    // Ritmo match = tiri totali attesi / media campionato tiri
    const avgShotsLg=(ld.avgHG+ld.avgAG)>0?ev.tiri.t/((lgAvgSplit(ts,'hsh','ash').h+lgAvgSplit(ts,'hsh','ash').a)||24):1;
    const ritmo=avgShotsLg>1.15?"Alto":avgShotsLg>0.95?"Medio":"Basso";
    const ritmoColor=avgShotsLg>1.15?P.ac:avgShotsLg>0.95?P.a3:P.a2;

    // Casa bonus = (home avg goals at home / overall avg) - 1
    const casaBonus=ld.avgHG>0?((lH/(ld.avgHG))-1)*100:0;

    // Best over/under events
    const bestEvents=[];
    Object.entries(ev).forEach(([key,e])=>{
      const cfg2=STAT_CFG[key];if(!cfg2)return;
      // Find the line closest to 50% (most actionable)
      const center=Math.round(e.t)-0.5;
      const pOv=1-poiCum(e.t,Math.floor(center));
      const label=pOv>=0.5?`${cfg2.label} O${center.toFixed(1)}`:`${cfg2.label} U${center.toFixed(1)}`;
      const prob=pOv>=0.5?pOv:1-pOv;
      bestEvents.push({label,prob});
    });
    // Add multigol
    if(bestMG)bestEvents.push({label:`MG ${bestMG.lb}`,prob:bestMG.p});
    bestEvents.sort((a,b)=>b.prob-a.prob);

    // Ref impact label
    const refImpact=ref?(ref.fpg!=null?(ref.fpg/(avgF||26)).toFixed(2):(ref.cpg/(avgY||4)).toFixed(2)):"N/A";

    return <>
      {/* Analisi Finale Match */}
      <Cd style={{gridColumn:"1 / -1",padding:0,overflow:"hidden"}}>
        <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"14px",background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#059669,#10B981)"}}>
          <span style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:800,color:"#fff",textTransform:"uppercase",letterSpacing:"0.06em"}}>Analisi Finale Match</span>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,color:"#ffffffcc",marginTop:4}}>Sintesi predittiva basata su tutte le metriche calcolate</div>
        </div>
        <div style={{padding:"16px 18px"}}>
          <div style={{padding:16,background:P.c3,borderRadius:10,borderLeft:`4px solid ${P.ac}`,marginBottom:14}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:800,color:P.tx,marginBottom:10}}>ANALISI PREVISIONALE COMPLETA</div>
            <div style={{fontSize:13,color:P.td,lineHeight:1.9}}>
              <p style={{margin:"0 0 10px"}}><b style={{color:P.tx}}>Scenario previsto:</b> {fav} {lvl}. Differenza xG: {lH.toFixed(2)} vs {lA.toFixed(2)}.</p>
              <p style={{margin:"0 0 10px"}}><b style={{color:P.tx}}>Gol attesi:</b> Il modello prevede <b style={{color:P.ac}}>{(lH+lA).toFixed(2)}</b> gol totali. Risultato più probabile: <b style={{color:P.ac}}>{topResult.h}-{topResult.a}</b>. Over 2.5 al <b>{(o25*100).toFixed(0)}%</b>, Under 2.5 al <b>{((1-o25)*100).toFixed(0)}%</b>. Over 1.5 al {(o15*100).toFixed(0)}%.</p>
              <p style={{margin:"0 0 10px"}}><b style={{color:P.tx}}>Entrambe segnano:</b> Probabilità {gg>0.5?"equilibrata":"sbilanciata"} tra GG ({(gg*100).toFixed(0)}%) e NG ({(ng*100).toFixed(0)}%).{gg>0.55?" Entrambe le squadre dovrebbero andare a segno.":""}</p>
              <p style={{margin:"0 0 10px"}}><b style={{color:P.tx}}>Risultati esatti più probabili:</b> {top3.map(r=>`${r.h}-${r.a} (${(r.p*100).toFixed(1)}%)`).join(", ")}.</p>
              <p style={{margin:"0 0 10px"}}><b style={{color:P.tx}}>Corner:</b> Previsti <b>{ev.corner.t.toFixed(1)}</b> corner totali ({ev.corner.eH.toFixed(1)} casa, {ev.corner.eA.toFixed(1)} trasferta). Over {(Math.round(ev.corner.t)-0.5).toFixed(1)} corner al <b>{((1-poiCum(ev.corner.t,Math.round(ev.corner.t)-1))*100).toFixed(0)}%</b>.</p>
              <p style={{margin:"0 0 10px"}}><b style={{color:P.tx}}>Disciplina:</b> Attesi <b>{Math.round(ev.falli.t)}</b> falli e <b>{ev.cartellini.t.toFixed(1)}</b> cartellini gialli. Over {(Math.round(ev.cartellini.t)-0.5).toFixed(1)} ammonizioni al <b>{((1-poiCum(ev.cartellini.t,Math.round(ev.cartellini.t)-1))*100).toFixed(0)}%</b>.{totalFouls>avgFoulsLg*1.1?<span style={{color:P.dg}}> Partita molto fisica.</span>:""}</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Eventi Più Probabili */}
          <div style={{padding:14,background:P.c3,borderRadius:10,marginBottom:14}}>
            <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,marginBottom:8}}>🎯 EVENTI PIÙ PROBABILI</div>
            {bestEvents.slice(0,4).map((e2,i)=>
              <div key={i} style={{display:"flex",alignItems:"center",gap:8,padding:"8px 10px",marginBottom:4,background:P.c2,borderRadius:6}}>
                <span style={{width:22,height:22,borderRadius:11,background:[P.ac,P.a2,"#8B5CF6",P.a3][i]||P.td,color:"#fff",fontSize:10,fontWeight:800,display:"flex",alignItems:"center",justifyContent:"center"}}>{i+1}</span>
                <span style={{flex:1,fontSize:13,color:P.tx}}>{e2.label}</span>
                <span style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:800,color:e2.prob>=0.6?P.ac:e2.prob>=0.5?P.a3:P.td}}>{(e2.prob*100).toFixed(0)}%</span>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Metriche Match */}
          <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(120px,1fr))",gap:8}}>
            <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,background:P.c3,borderRadius:8,borderBottom:`3px solid ${ritmoColor}`}}>
              <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:800,color:ritmoColor}}>{avgShotsLg.toFixed(2)}</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm,textTransform:"uppercase",fontWeight:600}}>Ritmo Match</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:11,color:ritmoColor}}>{ritmo}</div>
            </div>
            <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,background:P.c3,borderRadius:8,borderBottom:`3px solid ${casaBonus>0?P.ac:P.dg}`}}>
              <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:800,color:casaBonus>0?P.ac:P.dg}}>{casaBonus>0?"+":""}{casaBonus.toFixed(0)}%</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm,textTransform:"uppercase",fontWeight:600}}>Casa Bonus</div>
              <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.td}}>{home}</div>
            </div>
            <div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:12,background:P.c3,borderRadius:8,borderBottom:`3px solid ${stileColor}`}}>
              <div style={{fontSize:20,fontWeight:800,color:stileColor}}>{Math.round(totalFouls)}</div>

function calcIdx2(ref,ld){return ref.cpg/((ld.avgY||4))*100;}
