// ═══ SELF-CHECK SYSTEM ═══
function runHealthCheck(DATA){
const checks=[];
let ok=0,warn=0,fail=0;
// Check each league
Object.entries(LG).forEach(([k,cfg])=>{
const ld=DATA[k];
if(!ld){checks.push({id:k,label:`${cfg.fl} ${cfg.n}`,status:“fail”,msg:“Dati mancanti”});fail++;return;}
const nTeams=Object.keys(ld.ts||{}).length;
const nCal=(ld.cal||[]).length;
const nRef=(ld.ref||[]).length;
const nM=ld.nM||0;
// Check teams exist
if(nTeams<10){checks.push({id:k+”_teams”,label:`${cfg.fl} Squadre`,status:“fail”,msg:`Solo ${nTeams} squadre`});fail++;}
else{checks.push({id:k+”_teams”,label:`${cfg.fl} Squadre`,status:“ok”,msg:`${nTeams} squadre caricate`});ok++;}
// Check calendar match teams
const miss=new Set();
(ld.cal||[]).forEach(f=>{if(!ld.ts[f.h])miss.add(f.h);if(!ld.ts[f.a])miss.add(f.a);});
if(miss.size>0){checks.push({id:k+”_cal”,label:`${cfg.fl} Calendario`,status:“warn”,msg:`${miss.size} squadre non trovate: ${[...miss].slice(0,3).join(", ")}`});warn++;}
else if(nCal>0){checks.push({id:k+”_cal”,label:`${cfg.fl} Calendario`,status:“ok”,msg:`${nCal} partite`});ok++;}
else{checks.push({id:k+”_cal”,label:`${cfg.fl} Calendario`,status:“warn”,msg:“Nessuna partita”});warn++;}
// Check xG data
const noXg=Object.entries(ld.ts||{}).filter(([t,s])=>!s.xgNH||s.xgNH<5).length;
if(noXg>nTeams*0.3){checks.push({id:k+”_xg”,label:`${cfg.fl} Dati xG`,status:“warn”,msg:`${noXg}/${nTeams} squadre con dati xG insufficienti`});warn++;}
else{checks.push({id:k+”_xg”,label:`${cfg.fl} Dati xG`,status:“ok”,msg:`${nTeams-noXg}/${nTeams} squadre con xG completo`});ok++;}
// Check referees
if(nRef>0){checks.push({id:k+”_ref”,label:`${cfg.fl} Arbitri`,status:“ok”,msg:`${nRef} arbitri`});ok++;}
else{checks.push({id:k+”_ref”,label:`${cfg.fl} Arbitri`,status:“warn”,msg:“Nessun dato arbitri”});warn++;}
// Check averages are sane
if(ld.avgHG>0&&ld.avgHG<5&&ld.avgAG>0){checks.push({id:k+”_avg”,label:`${cfg.fl} Medie`,status:“ok”,msg:`${(ld.avgHG+ld.avgAG).toFixed(2)} gol/partita`});ok++;}
else{checks.push({id:k+”_avg”,label:`${cfg.fl} Medie`,status:“fail”,msg:“Medie campionato anomale”});fail++;}
});
// Check math engine
try{
const tp=poiP(1.5,2);
if(tp>0&&tp<1){checks.push({id:“math”,label:“Motore Poisson”,status:“ok”,msg:“Funzionante”});ok++;}
else throw new Error();
}catch(e){checks.push({id:“math”,label:“Motore Poisson”,status:“fail”,msg:“Errore nel calcolo”});fail++;}
// Check Dixon-Coles
try{
const tm=dcMatrix(1.5,1.0,-0.01);
if(tm&&tm[0]&&tm[0][0]>0){checks.push({id:“dc”,label:“Matrice Dixon-Coles”,status:“ok”,msg:“Funzionante”});ok++;}
else throw new Error();
}catch(e){checks.push({id:“dc”,label:“Matrice Dixon-Coles”,status:“fail”,msg:“Errore nel calcolo”});fail++;}
return{checks,ok,warn,fail,total:ok+warn+fail,score:Math.round(ok/(ok+warn+fail)*100)};
}

function HealthCheck({data,onDismiss}){
const[result,setResult]=useState(null);
const[step,setStep]=useState(0);
useEffect(()=>{
const r=runHealthCheck(data);
setResult(r);
const timer=setInterval(()=>setStep(s=>s>=r.total?r.total:s+1),80);
return()=>clearInterval(timer);
},[data]);
if(!result)return null;
const allDone=step>=result.total;
const statusColor=result.fail>0?P.dg:result.warn>2?P.a3:P.ac;
return <div style={{position:“fixed”,inset:0,zIndex:999,background:“rgba(8,12,20,0.95)”,display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,justifyContent:“center”,padding:20}}>
<div style={{maxWidth:480,width:“100%”,background:P.c1,borderRadius:16,border:`1px solid ${P.bd}`,overflow:“hidden”,boxShadow:“0 25px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)”}}>
{/* Header */}
<div style={{padding:“20px 24px”,background:`linear-gradient(135deg,${P.c2},${P.c1})`,borderBottom:`1px solid ${P.bd}`}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:12}}>
<span style={{fontSize:28}}>⚡</span>
<div>
<div style={{fontSize:18,fontWeight:800,background:`linear-gradient(135deg,${P.ac},${P.a2})`,WebkitBackgroundClip:“text”,WebkitTextFillColor:“transparent”}}>FAPro Self-Check</div>
<div style={{fontSize:12,color:P.tm}}>Verifica integrità dati e motore di calcolo</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
{/* Progress */}
<div style={{padding:“16px 24px”}}>
<div style={{height:4,background:P.c3,borderRadius:2,marginBottom:16,overflow:“hidden”}}>
<div style={{height:“100%”,width:`${(step/result.total)*100}%`,background:`linear-gradient(90deg,${P.ac},${P.a2})`,borderRadius:2,transition:“width 0.15s”}}/>
</div>
{/* Check items */}
<div style={{maxHeight:320,overflowY:“auto”,display:“flex”,flexDirection:“column”,gap:4}}>
{result.checks.slice(0,step).map((c,i)=>{
const ic=c.status===“ok”?“✅”:c.status===“warn”?“⚠️”:“❌”;
const col=c.status===“ok”?P.ac:c.status===“warn”?P.a3:P.dg;
return <div key={c.id} style={{display:“flex”,alignItems:“center”,gap:10,padding:“8px 12px”,borderRadius:8,background:P.c2,
animation:“fadeIn 0.3s ease-out”,opacity:1}}>
<span style={{fontSize:14,minWidth:20}}>{ic}</span>
<span style={{fontSize:12,fontWeight:600,color:P.tx,flex:1}}>{c.label}</span>
<span style={{fontSize:11,color:col}}>{c.msg}</span>
</div>;
})}
</div>
</div>
{/* Footer */}
{allDone&&<div style={{padding:“16px 24px”,borderTop:`1px solid ${P.bd}`,textAlign:“center”}}>
<div style={{display:“flex”,justifyContent:“center”,gap:20,marginBottom:14}}>
{[[“✅ OK”,result.ok,P.ac],[“⚠️ Avvisi”,result.warn,P.a3],[“❌ Errori”,result.fail,P.dg]].map(([lb,n,c])=>
<div key={lb} style={{textAlign:“center”}}>
<div style={{fontSize:22,fontWeight:800,color:c}}>{n}</div>
<div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>{lb}</div>
</div>)}
</div>
<div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:statusColor,marginBottom:12}}>
{result.fail===0&&result.warn===0?“Tutti i sistemi operativi — App pronta!”:
result.fail===0?`App funzionante con ${result.warn} avvisi minori`:
`${result.fail} problemi rilevati — Verifica i dati`}
</div>
<button onClick={onDismiss} style={{padding:“12px 36px”,borderRadius:10,border:“none”,cursor:“pointer”,fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,
background:`linear-gradient(135deg,${P.ac},${P.a2})`,color:P.bg,transition:“transform 0.2s”,boxShadow:`0 4px 15px ${P.ac}44`}}>
Avvia FAPro
</button>
</div>}
</div>

  </div>;
}

const allTeams=Object.keys(ld.ts||{});

      </button>)}

  <button onClick={()=>setShowCheck(true)} style={{background:"none",border:`1px solid ${P.bd}`,borderRadius:8,padding:"6px 10px",cursor:"pointer",fontSize:13,color:P.tm,transition:"all 0.2s"}} title="Self-Check">
    🩺
  </button>
  <button onClick={()=>setSidebar(true)} style={{background:P.c2,border:`1px solid ${P.bd}`,borderRadius:8,padding:"6px 10px",cursor:"pointer",fontSize:14,color:P.td,position:"relative",transition:"all 0.2s"}}>
    ⚙️
    {dynData&&<span style={{position:"absolute",top:-3,right:-3,width:8,height:8,borderRadius:4,background:P.ac}}/>}
  </button>
</div>

{/* Nav */}
<div style={{padding:"10px 16px",display:"flex",gap:4,borderBottom:`1px solid ${P.bd}22`,overflowX:"auto",background:`linear-gradient(180deg,${P.c1}88,transparent)`}}>
  {[["dashboard","📊 Dashboard"],["calendar","📅 Calendario"],["standings","🏆 Classifica"],["squadre","⚽ Squadre"],["referees","👤 Arbitri"]].map(([v,lb])=>
    <button key={v} onClick={()=>{setView(v);setFix(null);}}
      style={{background:view===v?`linear-gradient(135deg,${P.c2},${P.c3})`:"transparent",border:view===v?`1px solid ${P.bd}44`:"1px solid transparent",
        color:view===v?P.tx:P.tm,padding:"8px 16px",borderRadius:8,cursor:"pointer",fontSize:13,fontWeight:view===v?700:500,transition:"all 0.25s",whiteSpace:"nowrap",
        boxShadow:view===v?"0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2)":"none"}}>
      {lb}</button>)}
</div>

<div style={{padding:"14px 16px",maxWidth:1280,margin:"0 auto"}}>

  {view==="dashboard"&&<>
    <h2 style={hS}>📅 Prossime Partite — {LG[lg].n}</h2>
    <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fill,minmax(270px,1fr))",gap:10}}>
      {(ld.cal||[]).slice(0,12).map((f,i)=>{
        const sH2=ld.ts[f.h],sA2=ld.ts[f.a];
        const stH2=(ld.st||[]).find(s=>s.t===f.h),stA2=(ld.st||[]).find(s=>s.t===f.a);
        let qk=null;
        if(sH2&&sA2){const ql=quickLambdas(sH2,sA2,ld);
          qk=mkts(dcMatrix(ql.lH,ql.lA,ld.rho||0));
          if(ql.xg){qk.O25=ql.xg.pO25;qk.U25=ql.xg.pU25;qk.GG=ql.xg.pGG;qk.NG=ql.xg.pNG;}}
        return <Cd key={i} onClick={()=>openA(f)} style={{padding:14}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm,marginBottom:6,letterSpacing:"0.04em"}}>{f.d}</div>
          <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center"}}>
            <div><div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:14,marginBottom:2}}>{f.h}</div>{stH2&&<FB f={stH2.f}/>}</div>
            <div style={{color:P.tm,fontSize:12,fontWeight:700}}>vs</div>
            <div style={{textAlign:"right"}}><div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:14,marginBottom:2}}>{f.a}</div>{stA2&&<FB f={stA2.f}/>}</div></div>
          {qk&&<div style={{display:"flex",gap:6,marginTop:8}}>
            {[["1",P.ac],["X",P.a3],["2",P.a2]].map(([k,c])=>
              <div key={k} style={{flex:1,textAlign:"center",padding:"4px 0",borderRadius:4,background:P.c3}}>
                <div style={{fontSize:10,color:P.tm}}>{k}</div>
                <div style={{fontSize:14,fontWeight:700,color:c}}>{(qk[k]*100).toFixed(0)}%</div></div>)}
          </div>}
        </Cd>;})}
    </div>
    <h2 style={hS}>🏆 Classifica</h2>
    <Cd><StTb st={ld.st}/></Cd>
    <h2 style={hS}>📊 Statistiche Campionato</h2>
    <Cd><div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(130px,1fr))",gap:12}}>
      {[["Partite",ld.nM],["Gol/p",((ld.avgHG||0)+(ld.avgAG||0)).toFixed(2)],["Falli/p",(ld.avgF||0).toFixed(1)],
        ["Gialli/p",(ld.avgY||0).toFixed(2)],["Corner/p",(ld.avgC||0).toFixed(1)],["Squadre",allTeams.length]].map(([lb,v])=>
        <div key={lb} style={{padding:12,borderRadius:8,background:P.c3,textAlign:"center"}}>
          <div style={{fontSize:11,color:P.tm,marginBottom:4}}>{lb}</div>
          <div style={{fontSize:22,fontWeight:800,color:P.ac}}>{v}</div></div>)}
    </div></Cd>
  </>}

  {view==="calendar"&&<>
    <h2 style={hS}>📅 Calendario — {LG[lg].n}</h2>
    {Object.entries(calByDate).map(([dk,fxs])=><div key={dk} style={{marginBottom:16}}>
      <div style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:P.ac,padding:"6px 0",borderBottom:`1px solid ${P.bd}22`,marginBottom:8}}>{dk}</div>
      <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fill,minmax(270px,1fr))",gap:8}}>
        {fxs.map((f,i)=>{const tm=(f.d||"").split(" - ")[1]||"";
          return <Cd key={i} onClick={()=>openA(f)} style={{padding:12}}>
            <div style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",alignItems:"center"}}>
              <div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:14}}>{f.h}</div>
              <div style={{color:P.tm,fontSize:12,padding:"2px 8px",background:P.c3,borderRadius:4}}>{tm||"vs"}</div>
              <div style={{fontWeight:700,fontSize:14,textAlign:"right"}}>{f.a}</div></div>
          </Cd>;})}
      </div>
    </div>)}
  </>}

  {view==="standings"&&<>
    <h2 style={hS}>🏆 Classifica — {LG[lg].n}</h2>
    <Cd><StTb st={ld.st}/></Cd>
    <h2 style={hS}>⚡ Migliori Attacchi & Difese</h2>
    <div style={{display:"grid",gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(290px,1fr))",gap:14}}>
      <Cd><h3 style={ctS}>🔥 Attacchi (Casa)</h3>
        {allTeams.filter(t=>ld.ts[t].hg>2).sort((a,b)=>av(ld.ts[b].hgf,ld.ts[b].hg)-av(ld.ts[a].hgf,ld.ts[a].hg)).slice(0,8).map((t,i)=>
          <div key={t} style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",padding:"4px 0",borderBottom:`1px solid ${P.bd}11`}}>
            <span style={{fontSize:13,color:i<3?P.ac:P.tx}}>{i+1}. {t}</span>
            <span style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:P.ac}}>{av(ld.ts[t].hgf,ld.ts[t].hg).toFixed(2)}</span></div>)}
      </Cd>
      <Cd><h3 style={ctS}>🛡️ Difese (Trasferta)</h3>
        {allTeams.filter(t=>ld.ts[t].ag>2).sort((a,b)=>av(ld.ts[a].aga,ld.ts[a].ag)-av(ld.ts[b].aga,ld.ts[b].ag)).slice(0,8).map((t,i)=>
          <div key={t} style={{display:"flex",justifyContent:"space-between",padding:"4px 0",borderBottom:`1px solid ${P.bd}11`}}>
            <span style={{fontSize:13,color:i<3?P.ac:P.tx}}>{i+1}. {t}</span>
            <span style={{fontSize:13,fontWeight:700,color:P.w}}>{av(ld.ts[t].aga,ld.ts[t].ag).toFixed(2)}</span></div>)}
      </Cd>
    </div>
  </>}

  {view==="squadre"&&<><h2 style={hS}>⚽ Statistiche Squadre — {LG[lg].n}</h2><TeamSection ld={ld}/></>}

  {view==="referees"&&<RefSection ld={ld}/>}

  {view==="analysis"&&fix&&<Analysis fix={fix} ld={ld} onBack={()=>setView("calendar")}/>}
</div>

<div style={{textAlign:"center",padding:"24px 16px",color:P.tm,fontSize:11,borderTop:`1px solid ${P.bd}22`,marginTop:30,
  background:`linear-gradient(180deg,transparent,${P.c1}44)`}}>

  </div>;
}
